        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-王菲英语语法-第十四季" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#王菲英语语法-第十四季"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>王菲英语语法 第十四季</h1>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">笔记更新地址:  <a href="https://github.com/Eished/wfyyyf_notes">https://github.com/Eished/wfyyyf_notes</a></p>
</blockquote>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-语法基础概念1098完美语法体系" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#语法基础概念1098完美语法体系"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>语法基础概念（10+9+8完美语法体系）</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-十种词性" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#十种词性"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>十种词性</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>介词 Prepositions</li>
<li>冠词 Articles</li>
<li>名词 Nouns</li>
<li>代词 Pronouns</li>
<li>数词 Numerals</li>
<li>副词 Adverbs</li>
<li>形容词 Adjectives</li>
<li>动词 Verbs</li>
<li>连词 Conjunctions</li>
<li>感叹词（只有叹词没有语法内容）</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-九种句子成分" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#九种句子成分"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>九种句子成分</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>主语 Subject</li>
<li>谓语 Predicate Verb</li>
<li>宾语 Object</li>
<li>表语 Predicative（主语补语）</li>
<li>双宾</li>
<li>宾补 Object Complement</li>
<li>定语 Attributive</li>
<li>状语 Adverbial</li>
<li>同位语 Appositive</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-八种句式" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#八种句式"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>八种句式</h3>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420224004676.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420224004676.png" alt="image-20210420224004676" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>五种基本句型源于动词性质</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>五种基础简单句</strong> Simple Sentence
<ol dir="auto">
<li>主 + 谓 + 宾</li>
<li>主 + 系 + 表</li>
<li>主 + 谓 + 双宾</li>
<li>主 + 谓 + 宾补</li>
<li>主 + 谓</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>三种高级复合句</strong> Complex Sentence 复杂句
<ol dir="auto">
<li>名词性从句
<ol dir="auto">
<li>主语从句</li>
<li>宾语从句</li>
<li>表语从句</li>
<li>同位语从句</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>定语从句</li>
<li>状语从句</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420225507792.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420225507792.png" alt="image-20210420225507792" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-王菲语法树" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#王菲语法树"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>王菲语法树</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>名词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>单复数</li>
<li>所有格</li>
<li>主谓一致</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>代词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>形式</li>
<li>含义</li>
<li>用法</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>数词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>基数词</li>
<li>序数词</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>冠词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>定冠词</li>
<li>不定冠词</li>
<li>零冠词</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>形容词，副词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>三级</li>
<li>固定句型</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>介词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>用法</li>
<li>分类</li>
<li>功能</li>
<li>固定搭配</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>动词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>时态</li>
<li>语态</li>
<li>非谓语动词</li>
<li>虚拟语气</li>
<li>独立主格结构</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>连词</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>并列连词</li>
<li>从属连词（三大从句）</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>其它</strong>：
<ol dir="auto">
<li>强调句</li>
<li>倒装句</li>
<li>反义疑问句</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-基本概念---简单句重要" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#基本概念---简单句重要"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>基本概念 - 简单句（重要）</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>陈述句（五种句型）</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>主语 + 系动词 + 表语</strong>（系动词后面叫表语）
<ul dir="auto">
<li>London is the capital of England.</li>
<li>系动词:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>be 动词</li>
<li>感官动词（与五官相关单词）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>主语 + 谓语</strong>（动词是<strong>不及物动词</strong>，不能加宾语）
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I get up early in the morning.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>主语 + 谓语 + 宾语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I love watermelon.</li>
<li>表语/宾语本质相同
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>动词后面叫宾语</strong></li>
<li>两种特殊动词后面叫表语</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>主 + 谓 + 双宾</strong>（直接宾语+间接宾语）
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The rabbit showed <em>us</em> a <em>carrot</em>.</li>
<li>改成被动句，会出现两个被动句
<ul dir="auto">
<li>us 和 carrot 都可以做被动语态的主语</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>主 + 谓 + 宾语 + 宾补</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They elected <em>Martin</em> their monitor.</li>
<li>改成被动句只有一个被动句
<ul dir="auto">
<li>只有 Martin 能做被动语态主语</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>陈述句形式</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>肯定式</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Honesty is the best policy.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>否定式</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She will not listen to me.</li>
<li>l don' t think it right.</li>
<li>在助动词后面加 not , 不能直接加动词后面</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>一般疑问句</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>可以用 yes/no 回答</li>
<li>陈述句变一般疑问句有<strong>三种类型</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>提前系动词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>陈述句: 主语 + 系动词 + 表语</li>
<li>疑问句: 系动词 + 主语 + 表语</li>
<li>You were coming with us.</li>
<li>Were you coming with us？ -Yes</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>提前助动词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>陈述句: 主语 + 谓语 + (宾语)</li>
<li>疑问句: 助动词 + 主语 + 动词原形 + 其它
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>助动词</strong>: 帮助动词的动词 (完成<strong>语态/时态/疑问/否定</strong>) 无词义</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>You <em>have found</em> a new job.</li>
<li><em>Have</em> you <em>found</em> a new job yet？
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Yes, I have/No, I haven 't.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>提前情态动词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>陈述句: 主语 + 情态动词 + 动词原形 + 其它</li>
<li>疑问句: 情态动词 + 主语 + 动词原形 + 其它
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>情态动词</strong>和<strong>助动词</strong>都<strong>不能</strong>单独充当<strong>谓语</strong>, 必须和动词放在一起充当谓语</li>
<li><strong>情态动词</strong>: 有词义; <strong>助动词</strong>: 无词义</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>You <em>can solve</em> this problem</li>
<li><em>Can</em> you <em>solve</em> this problem？
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Yes I can/No, l can’t.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>特殊疑问句</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">以特殊疑问词开头；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">对句中某一成分提问；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">不能用 Yes/No 进行回答</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Who - 提问人</th>
<th>Where - 提问地点</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Whose - 提问所属</td>
<td>Why - 提问原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Whom - 提问宾格人</td>
<td>How - 提问方式或数量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>What - 提问事情或属性</td>
<td>How much/many - 提问数量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When - 提问时间</td>
<td>Which - 提问选择</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">特殊疑问句 例句1</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Who were you on the phone with？</li>
<li>Jim.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">特殊疑问句 例句2</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Whom is he dating？</li>
<li>He is dating Anna.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>选择疑问句</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">选择疑问句<strong>用 or 连接</strong>；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">提出两个或两个以上的句式供选择；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">选择疑问句不能用 Yes/No 回答。</p>
<p dir="auto">选择疑问句 例句1</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Do you like chocolate or vanilla better？</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">选择疑问句 例句2</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Are you going to drive or do you want me to？</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>反义疑问句</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">陈述句部分是<strong>肯定句</strong>，疑问句部分用<strong>否定句</strong>；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">陈述句部分是<strong>否定句</strong>，反意疑问句用<strong>肯定句</strong>。</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>前肯后否；前否后肯</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>反义疑问句</strong> 例句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is your teacher, isn’t he?</li>
<li>You found the key in the bedroom, didn’t you？</li>
<li>The boy has to clean his room, doesn’t he?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>感叹句</strong>的反义疑问句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>一律用<strong>否定式提问</strong></li>
<li>What a clever boy, isn’t he?</li>
<li>What a lovely day, isn't it？</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>祈使句</strong>的反义疑问句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>用 <strong>will you</strong></li>
<li>Let’s 开始, 用 <strong>shall we</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>含 must</strong> 的反义疑问句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>表“必须”</strong>：反意疑问句为 mustn't…？/ needn't…?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He must study hard at English, mustn 't he？/neednt he?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>表推测“一定，肯定”</strong>：反意疑问句与 must 后面的<strong>动词</strong>呼应
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You must be joking, aren't you?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>含否定词</strong>的反义疑问句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>常见否定词：hardly; never; seldom; little; few; nowhere; nothing 等</li>
<li>反意疑问句用<strong>肯定提问</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Frank hardly goes to parties, does he?</li>
<li>He has few triends, has he?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>复合句</strong>的反义疑问句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>复合句的反意疑问句都<strong>对主句提问</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>复合句: 两个以上句子构成, 从句连词的三大从句</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>He was punished <em>because</em> he violated the regulation, wasn 't he？</li>
<li>You never told me <em>that</em> you had been ill, did you?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>宾语从句</strong>的反义疑问句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I don' t think/ suppose/ believe/ imagine 引导的<strong>宾语从句</strong>，反意疑问句应<strong>与从句的主语，谓语部分一致</strong>，用<strong>肯定式的提问</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>中英文否定词位置不一致, 否定词转移</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I don' t suppose anyone will volunteer, will they?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我相信没人会做 否定词属于后面从句</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I don' t believe she has done it, has she?</li>
<li>我相信她没做这件事, 否定词属于后面从句</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>感叹句</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>What 感叹句</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>What + a/an + 形容词 + <strong>可数名词单数</strong> + [主语 + 谓语]！</li>
<li>What + a/an + <strong>名词</strong> + 主语 + 谓语！</li>
<li>What + 形容词 + <strong>不可数名词/复数名词</strong> + [主语 + 谓语]！
<ul dir="auto">
<li>What a marvelous sight!</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>How 感叹句</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>How + <strong>形容词/副词</strong> + [主语 + 谓语]！</li>
<li>How + <strong>形容词</strong> + a/an + 可数名词单数 + [主语 + 谓语]!
<ul dir="auto">
<li>How noble of him to do that !</li>
<li>How intelligent you are！</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>语气词/感叹号</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Oh, I am depressed!</li>
<li>I cannot survive without you!</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>祈使句</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>没有主语, 通常用动词开头</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表示命令
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Please sit down.</li>
<li>Leave this place at once.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表示请求或祝愿
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Have a safe trip！</li>
<li>Let's go for a walk.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201025225320224.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201025225320224.png" alt="image-20201025225320224" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201025225349111.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201025225349111.png" alt="image-20201025225349111" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-一名词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#一名词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>一、名词</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-11-名词的分类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#11-名词的分类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.1 名词的分类</h3>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-111-专有名词普通名词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#111-专有名词普通名词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.1.1 专有名词&amp;普通名词</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>专有名词</strong>：特定的某人、地方或机构等专有的名称。</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">人名：Tom, Smith, Jackie, Wang</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">地名：Beijing, Virginia, London.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">国家名：China, Rusa, Pakistan.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">单位名：the State Council, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Finance.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">组织名：IMF ASEAN EU OPEC</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">大型活动或事件：The Belt and Road, BCIKS</p>
<p dir="auto">注意专有名词第一个字母要大写</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>普通名词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>可数名词</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>个体名词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>aunt, uncle</li>
<li>表个体</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>集体名词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>class, army</li>
<li>表人或事物的总称</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>不可数名词</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>物质名词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Coffee, water</li>
<li>无法分为个体的事物</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>抽象名词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>interesting, pleasure</li>
<li>表性质 / 状态 / 情感 等抽象概念</li>
<li>前一般不加定冠词</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>语言名词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Chinese, French</li>
<li>表语言名称</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-112-可数名词不可数名词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#112-可数名词不可数名词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.1.2 可数名词&amp;不可数名词</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>例句
<ul dir="auto">
<li>可数: Most classrooms have computers.</li>
<li>不可数: They left the house to go for a walk after tea.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>注意:
<ol dir="auto">
<li>不可数名词, 不可数字计算</li>
<li>不可数名词, **不加不定冠词 ** (a/an) 与数词；</li>
<li>不可数名词, 可<strong>加定冠词</strong> (the)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>家具（furniture）
We have too much furniture.</li>
<li>设备（ equipment）
The plant was dismantled of all its equipment and furniture.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-113-具体名词抽象名词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#113-具体名词抽象名词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.1.3 具体名词&amp;抽象名词</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>具体名词</strong>：指可以看到，听到，闻到，触摸到的事物。
<ol dir="auto">
<li>人物：man, Mrs. Jones</li>
<li>地点：river, London</li>
<li>事物：book, mountains, sports car</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>抽象名词</strong>：指代情感，观念，想法等无形的事物的名词。
<ol dir="auto">
<li>例: love, happiness, intelligence, anger, excitement</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-114-复数形式出现的名词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#114-复数形式出现的名词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.1.4 复数形式出现的名词</h4>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">单词</th>
<th align="left">例句</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">scIssors 剪刀</td>
<td align="left">There are three pairs of scissors in the drawer.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">tweezers 镊子</td>
<td align="left">Could you pass me those tweezers？</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">binoculars 望远镜</td>
<td align="left">She gave me some binoculars.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">glasses 眼睛</td>
<td align="left">I've lost my glasses!</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">clothes 衣服</td>
<td align="left">She put her clothes in the suitcase.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">congratulations 祝贺</td>
<td align="left">Many congratulations!</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-12-名词的单复数" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#12-名词的单复数"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.2 名词的单复数</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>规则名词</strong>的复数形式</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>-s 例如：大多数名词在单数名词后加 -s
<ul dir="auto">
<li>desk→ desks day→days house→ houses</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>-es 例如：<strong>以 o, s, x, ch, sh 结尾的单数名词后加 -es</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>hero→ heroes, bush→ bushes, fox→ foxes</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>以 -y 结尾</strong>的名词
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>辅音 +y 的名词，变 y 为 i 加 -es</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>city&gt; cities</li>
<li>country→&gt; countries</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>元音 +y 的名词，加 -s</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>boy→&gt;boys</li>
<li>donkey &gt;donkeys</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>-f, -fe 结尾</strong>的名词
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>变 f 为 v 加 -es</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>half, life, leaf, loaf, knife, shelf, wife</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>直接加 -s</strong> （没规律只能背诵）
<ul dir="auto">
<li>belief, grief, cliff, gulf, roof, proof</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>特殊情况
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>-ch 结尾发 /k/ 音, 加 -s</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>monarch（君主）→ monarchs</li>
<li>stomach（胃）→ stomachs</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>“元音+o” 或 “oo” 结尾的词，加 “-s”</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>bamboo → bamboos</li>
<li>portfolio → portfolios</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>注意:</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>有的 “o” 结尾，加 “es”, 辅音结尾</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>cargo, echo, embargo, hero, tomato, veto</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>有的 “o” 结尾，加 “-s”, 辅音结尾</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>memento, concerto, piano, solo, photo, quarto, kilo, largo</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>**有的 o 结尾，加 “es” 或 “s” **
<ul dir="auto">
<li>zero, volcano, mango, archipelago banjo, grotto, halo</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>不规则名词</strong>的复数形式</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>man-men</th>
<th>child-children</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>woman-women</td>
<td>fish-fish</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>goose-geese</td>
<td>deer-deer</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>foot-foot</td>
<td>sheep-sheep</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>tooth-teeth</td>
<td>mouse-mice</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>复合名词</strong>的复数形式</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>不可数名词-结尾，无复数形式</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>homework, newspaper</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>man 或 woman为前缀的，前后名词都变复数</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>woman doctor → women doctors</li>
<li>man waiter → men waiters</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>两个名词构成</strong>的（前面的名词为man或 woman除外），<strong>后面名词变复数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>boy friend → boy friends</li>
<li>paper bag → paper bags</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>“<strong>可数名词 + 介词</strong>（短语）” <strong>前面名词变复数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>father-in-law → fathers-in-law : 岳父</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>动词/过去分词 + 副词</strong>，<strong>副词加s</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>grown-up → grown-ups,</li>
<li>stand-by → stand-bys</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-13-所有格" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#13-所有格"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.3 所有格</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>英语名词有三个格，即主格、宾格和所有格。(名词的主格宾格相同)</li>
<li>它分 “s” 所有格和 “of“ 印所有格两种形式。</li>
<li>表所属关系，即“…的”。</li>
</ul>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>‘s 所有格</strong> (中英语序一致)
<ol dir="auto">
<li>构成
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>单数名词</strong>/复数名词<strong>非 s 结尾</strong>，后加 ‘s;</li>
<li><strong>复数名词 s 结尾</strong>, 加 ‘
<ul dir="auto">
<li>boys' school 男子学校</li>
<li>the Smiths'car 史密斯家的小汽车</li>
<li>the boss's plan 老板的计划</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>带<strong>词尾 -s 的单数名词</strong>后，通常仍加 -‘s。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the boss's plan老板的计划</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用 and 连接的<strong>并列名词的所有格</strong>要分两种情况。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>表示<strong>各自的所有关系</strong>时，要分别在并列名词后加 ‘s</li>
<li>表示<strong>共同的所有关系</strong>时，只在最后一个名词后加 ‘s
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tom's and Jim‘s rooms. 汤姆和吉姆（各自）的房间。</li>
<li>Tom and jim’s room. 汤姆和吉姆（共同）的房间。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用法
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>时间后</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>this month’s schedule 这个月的日程表</li>
<li>10 day‘s holiday 十天的假期</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>国家或城市后</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>China‘s policy 中国的政策</li>
<li>the town’s population 这个镇的人</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>组织机构后</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the station' s waiting-room 车站候车室</li>
<li>the newspaper' s editorial policy 这家报纸的编辑方针</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>度量衡后</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a kilo’s weight 1千克的重量</li>
<li>1000 pound‘s price 1000磅的价钱</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>天体后</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the moon‘s light 月光</li>
<li>Jupiter’s size 木星的大小</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>of 所有格</strong> (中英语序相反)
<ol dir="auto">
<li>修饰前面的名词;</li>
<li>表两个名词间的所属关系。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The content of the website.</li>
<li>A friend of mine told me that all of the tickets have already sold out.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>双重所有格</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>of + 名词 ′s 所有格;</li>
<li>of + 名词性物主代词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is a friend of mine.</li>
<li>This is a photo of my mother.</li>
<li>This is a photo of my mother’s.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-14-主谓一致" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#14-主谓一致"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.4 主谓一致</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">集合名词做主语</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表<strong>整体概念</strong>，<strong>谓语动词用复数</strong>；</li>
<li>表<strong>个体概念</strong>，<strong>谓语动词用单数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The whole family is active. 个体概念</li>
<li>The family have met their various obligations. 整体概念</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>单复数同形名词</strong>做主语：<strong>根据句义</strong>，判断谓语动词的单复数。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We need to find some other means of transportation.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们得找其他交通工具了。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>国名、组织机构、书名、报刊名</strong>等复数形式的专有名词作为整体对待，谓语<strong>用单数</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The United Nations has passed a resolution to lift sanctions against Iraq.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>联合国通过了解除对伊制裁的决定。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The Times reports the news of the strike.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>时代杂志报导了罢工的消息。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Great Expectations was written by Dickens in 1860.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>《远大前程》是狄更斯于1860年写的。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>由 and 或 both… and… 连接两个单数名词</strong>作主语时，指代复数概念，谓语动词<strong>用复数</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She and her friends are at the fair.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她和她的朋友在会上。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>and 连接的两个词<strong>指同一个人</strong>、同一事物或同一概念，且两个名词<strong>共用一个冠词</strong>，谓语动词必须<strong>用单数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The teacher and writer is her friend.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这位教师兼作家是她的朋友</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>and 连接<strong>单数主语</strong>前如有 <strong>every, each, no, many a</strong> 修饰时，谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>No smoking or drinking is allowed. Every man and woman is required to check in.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>不许抽烟、饮酒。按要求，毎位男性及女性需要登记。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>时间，距离，金钱，价格</strong>等常<strong>作为整体</strong>看待时，谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>形式</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Five dollars is a lot of money.</li>
<li>Fifteen miles is not a long way.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>就近原则</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>there (客观存在, 有) / here be 句型 (倒装结构, 谓语在前, 主语在后)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There are many possible candidates.</li>
<li>Here are some stones.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>or, either...or…(二选一)， neither... nor…(两者都不)，not only... but（also）连接并列成分作主语。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>His friends or <strong>the boy</strong> runs every day.</li>
<li>Neither gray nor <strong>white</strong> is my favorite color.</li>
<li>Either Grandpa or my <strong>sisters</strong> are going to the park.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>就远原则</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>as well as (…和…, 除了…还有…);</li>
<li>together / along / combined with;</li>
<li>rather than; except; besides; including;</li>
<li>in addition to; apart from.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>The politician</strong>, along with the newsmen, is on the meeting.</li>
<li><strong>Excitement</strong>, as well as nervousness, is the cause of her shaking.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>some of, plenty of, a lot of, lots of, most of, the rest of, all of, half of, part of，分数、百分数 + of + 名词短语作主语</strong>，谓语动常<strong>与 of 后的名词保持数的一致</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>All of the <strong>chicken</strong> is gone.</li>
<li>Most of the <strong>cookies</strong> were eaten.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">在<strong>四则运算</strong>中，谓语动词多<strong>用单数</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>18 minus 12 is 6.</li>
<li>Two and two is four.</li>
<li>Four times four divided by two is eight.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">“a number of + 可数名词复数” 谓语动词<strong>用复数</strong>； 许多,大量</p>
<p dir="auto">“the number of + 可数名词” 谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>。…的数量</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>A number of</strong> students were late for class.</li>
<li><strong>The number of</strong> students in the class is fifteen.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">"<strong>each, one, no one, some(any, no, every) + body(one 或 ething)</strong>” 作主语或作限定词，谓语动词<strong>单数</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Each</strong> gets a trophy for playing.</li>
<li><strong>Somebody</strong> will pay for this.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">“one and a half + 复数名词”作主语，谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>。大于等于 2 用复数</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>One and a half</strong> apples is left on the table.</li>
<li><strong>One and a half</strong> hours is not enough.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">“a/an + <strong>单数名词</strong> + or two” 作主语，谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>。</p>
<p dir="auto">one or two + <strong>复数名词</strong>作主语，谓语动词<strong>用复数</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>A student</strong> or two has failed the exam.</li>
<li>One or <strong>two suggestions</strong> were recommended.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">many a…或 more than one + 名词作主语，谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>。用单数名词代表许多,大量</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Many a</strong> man thinks life is meaningless without purpose.</li>
<li><strong>More than one</strong> student has tried this.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">“one + of + 复数名词” 结构中，谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>动词。群体中之一</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>One of</strong> the students in our class is from the UK.</li>
<li><strong>One of</strong> their daughters has just had a baby.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">few, many, several, all, some后加名词作主语，谓语动词<strong>用复数</strong>。</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Both</strong> are qualified for the job.</li>
<li><strong>Many</strong> went to the beach and got sunburned.</li>
<li><strong>Few</strong> know what it really takes to get ahead.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201025225613928.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201025225613928.png" alt="image-20201025225613928" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026001831570.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026001831570.png" alt="image-20201026001831570" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-二代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#二代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>二、代词</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>指代</strong>已经提到的或即将提到的人或物。</li>
<li><strong>代替</strong>所提到的名词或名词性短语。</li>
<li>在句中可做<strong>主语</strong>，<strong>宾语</strong>，<strong>表语</strong>或<strong>同位语</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It <strong>is</strong> a table.（<strong>主语</strong>）</li>
<li>I asked <strong>myself</strong> what i would have done in such a situation. (<strong>宾语</strong>)</li>
<li>The boys <strong>all</strong> laughed their heads oft.（<strong>同位语</strong>）</li>
<li>Who’s <strong>that</strong>？（<strong>表语</strong>）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-21-人称代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#21-人称代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.1 人称代词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">定义</p>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026140251750.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026140251750.png" alt="image-20201026140251750" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">人称代词的句法作用</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>做主语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>I</strong> asked my mother if she'd lend me some money, but she said no.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>做宾语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Neither of <strong>us</strong> forgot about it.</li>
<li>ls sam there？ Let me talk to <strong>him</strong>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作表语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>That must be <strong>her</strong> now.</li>
<li>Who is <strong>it</strong>？</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>it 的用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>指上文提及的某一物体、动物或其他事物。</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The company was losing money and it had to let people go.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>尚不知性别的婴儿</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She could compel him to support the child after it was born.</li>
<li>Her baby's due next month. She hopes it will be a boy.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>指时间、距离、天气或环境等。</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's ten past twelve.</li>
<li>It's time for lunch.</li>
<li>It is raining.</li>
<li>It 's two miles to the beach.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>指已经发生或正在发生的事件或情况。</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>When the factory closes, it will mean 500 people losing their jobs.</li>
<li>Stop it, you're hurting me！</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>识别、分辨人</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's your mother on the phone.</li>
<li>Hello, Peter, it's Mike here.</li>
<li>Was it you who put these books on my desk？</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>强调句</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It' s spain that they're going to, not Portugal.</li>
<li>It was three weeks later that he heard the news.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026141619937.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026141619937.png" alt="image-20201026141619937" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-22-物主代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#22-物主代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.2 物主代词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">定义</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>形容词性物主代词</strong>; + n = 名词性物主代词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Anyone who drives his car at 100 miles an hour is asking for trouble.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>名词性物主代词（请背诵表格）</strong> ; 避免名词重复出现
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He' s a friend <strong>of</strong> mine (= one of my friends). 双重所有格</li>
<li>Which table is ours？</li>
<li>I think she's a relation of theirs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">句法作用</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">形容词性物主代词：句中<strong>做定语</strong>，<strong>修饰名词</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Your mother is driving me crazy.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">注意：在<strong>动名词</strong>的复合结构中，形容词性物主代词做名词的<strong>逻辑主语</strong>。等同于定语从句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She was somewhat surprised at <strong>my asking</strong> (= that I asked) for the book to be returned.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">名词性物主代词</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>主语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Ours is the red car parked over there.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>表语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Whose bag is this？ It's mine.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>宾语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Let's go back to yours after the show.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-23-反身代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#23-反身代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.3 反身代词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">表“自己。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">有人称和数的变化。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Be careful with that knife or you’ll cut yourself！</li>
<li>They asked themselves where they had gone wrong.</li>
</ul>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">人称</th>
<th align="center">单数</th>
<th align="center">复数</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">第一人称</td>
<td align="center">myself</td>
<td align="center">ourselves</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">第二人称</td>
<td align="center">yourself</td>
<td align="center">yourselves</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">第三人称</td>
<td align="center">himself / herself / itself</td>
<td align="center">themselves</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026150046024.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026150046024.png" alt="image-20201026150046024" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-24-指示代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#24-指示代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.4 指示代词</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">this, that, these, those 做代词时为指示代词；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表“这个，那个，这些，那些”；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">在句中做主语，宾语。</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>单数</th>
<th>this</th>
<th>that</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>复数</td>
<td>these</td>
<td>those</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">句法作用</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>做主语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>These are too heavy for me to carry.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>做宾语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I like this better than that.</li>
<li>I don' t say no to that.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作定语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Can I help you with those bags？</li>
<li>I've never liked that cousin of hers.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作表语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Who's that？ Is that the girl you told me about?</li>
<li>What's this？Is this what you're looking for？</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">用法</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">this 和 these 指在时间或空间上<strong>较近的人或物</strong>，</p>
<p dir="auto">that 和 those 指在时间或空间上<strong>较远的人或者事物</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This is a pen and that’s an eraser.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">为避免重复，用 that 或 those 来代替<strong>前面已提到</strong>的人或物；</p>
<p dir="auto">用 this 或 these 来代替<strong>下文中将要提</strong>的人或物。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She's very friendly and that is why we all love her.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>打电话</strong>介绍自己时用 <strong>this 指 “我”</strong>，不用 l;</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>询问对方</strong>用 <strong>that 指 “你”</strong>，不用 you。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Hello. This is Mary. Who's that？</li>
<li>This is tom.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-25-关系代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#25-关系代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.5 关系代词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">用来<strong>引导定语从句</strong>；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">在从句中<strong>充当一定的句子成分</strong>；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">关系代词有<strong>主格</strong>，<strong>宾格</strong>和<strong>属格</strong>之分;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">有指人与指物之分。</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>指人</th>
<th>who, whom, whose, that, as</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>指物</td>
<td>which, whose, that, as</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-26-连接代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#26-连接代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.6 连接代词</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>疑问代词</strong>在引导<strong>从句</strong>时，称为连接代词。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>who, whom whose, what, which whoever, whomever whichever, whatever</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-27-不定代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#27-不定代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.7 不定代词</h3>
<p dir="auto">不定代词指代情况不详的人或物。</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>合成不定代词</strong> : 复合不定代词</p>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026153359446.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026153359446.png" alt="image-20201026153359446" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">第二类不定代词</p>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026153624088.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026153624088.png" alt="image-20201026153624088" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>合成不定代词<strong>谓语动词用单数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There's something sharp in my shoes.</li>
<li>Nobody agrees with me.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>-thing 结尾指物</strong>；<strong>-one, -body 结尾指人</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Everyone involved in the accident has been questioned by the police.</li>
<li>She could be anything（= any age） between 30 and 40.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>合成不定代词
<ol dir="auto">
<li>只能作<strong>主语</strong>、<strong>宾语</strong>或<strong>表语</strong>，不能作定语；</li>
<li><strong>some-， every-</strong> 开头的不定代词用在<strong>肯定句中</strong>;</li>
<li><strong>any-</strong> 常用在<strong>否定句与疑问句</strong>汇中；</li>
<li><strong>no-</strong> 用在<strong>否定句</strong>中。</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">合成不定代词句法功能</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>做主语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Anybody can use the pool—you don't need to be a member.</li>
<li>Somebody in the office will know.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>做宾语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The terrorists forced everybody to lie face down on the floor.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>主+谓+宾+宾补+地点状语</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>You can't blame him for everything.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作表语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A first I thought there was no one in the room.</li>
<li>There' s never anything worth watching on TV.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>与 else 连用</strong>：已经谈及一人或物，又想再提到另外的人或物，可在<strong>合成不定代词后加 -else”</strong> , 其余的 / 另外的
<ol dir="auto">
<li>You'll have to ask someone else.</li>
<li>There's nothing else we can do to help.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>注意
<ol dir="auto">
<li>合成不定代词<strong>前不能加定语</strong></li>
<li>如表示限定，需在<strong>其后加限定词</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>an important somebody （x）</li>
<li>somebody important （v）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>常用短语 (背诵)</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>anything but</strong> = definitely not ; 绝不</li>
<li><strong>be/have nothing to do with somebody /something</strong> = to have no connection with somebody/something ; 和人/事无关</li>
<li><strong>nothing but</strong> = only； no more /less than ; 只是, 肯定句</li>
<li><strong>nothing like（informal 非正式）</strong>= not at all like not nearly /not at all ;</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>many, much, more, most, few, little用法（请背诵）</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>a 肯定, 没 a 否定; 小(little) 不可数;</strong></p>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026161348455.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026161348455.png" alt="image-20201026161348455" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>some, any, either 用法 (请背诵)</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>some 用</strong>于<strong>肯定句</strong>中，表示一些。
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Some lucky person will win more than $1,000,000 in the competition.</li>
<li>Some have compared his work to Picasso's.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>any 用法</strong>：用<strong>否定句，疑问句</strong>。
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表 “一点儿，若干”
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There was hardly any food left by the time we got there.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们到那儿的时候，几乎一点儿吃的都没了。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表 “任何一个，无论哪个”
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Any of you should be able to answer this question.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我希望他再也不要给我们添任何麻烦了。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表 “略微，稍微”
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Can't you run any faster？
<ul dir="auto">
<li>不是所有单词能放到比较级之前</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Those trousers don't look any different from the others.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>那条裤子看起来和其他裤子没什么两样</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>either 用法</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>否定句</strong>中代表 also 或 too，表 “也”。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They do really good food at that restaurant and it 's not very expensive either.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>那家餐厅饭菜做得很好，而且价格也不太贵。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>“<strong>要么…要么</strong>，不是…就是，<strong>（两者中）任何一个</strong>”
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Either candidate would be ideal for the job.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这两个人哪一个都是做这项工作的理想人选</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Either you leave now or I call the police!
<ul dir="auto">
<li>要么你现在离开，要么我就叫警察！</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>all, both, each, every用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>all 的用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">“每一个，<strong>全部</strong>，所有”，<strong>修饰可数名词</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>All animals have to eat in order to live.</li>
<li>The cast all lined up on stage to take their bow.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>全体演员都在台上站成一排向观众鞠躬。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>“完全地”</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The downstairs rooms were painted all in greens and blues.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>楼下的房间全都粉刷成了绿色和蓝色。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>固定搭配</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>all in all</strong> : 总的说来，从各方面来说；总之</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>all but</strong> : 几乎，差不多</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>all round</strong> : 全面地，在各方面</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">注意：<strong>all 后面不能加 "the"</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>both 用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表 “两个，两者”</li>
<li>句中作主语，定语，宾语，同位语。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Both my parents are teachers.</li>
<li>Would you like milk or sugar or both？</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表 “两者都…” 时，用 ”both…and” 结构。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Both men and women have complained about the advertisement.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>男人和女人都抱怨过这个广告。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>each 用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>each 表 “<strong>每一个</strong>”，可做主语，宾语，定语以及同位语。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We each（= every one of us） wanted the bedroom with the balcony, so we tossed a coin to decide. 主语
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们大家都想住那间带阳台的卧室，所以只好扔硬币来决定</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Each answer is worth 20 points. 定语
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每个答案值20分。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>every 用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表 <strong>“每一个” + 单数名词</strong>，不单独使用。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Every player wants to be in a winning team.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每一名玩家都想待在一个能赢的队伍里。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Every cook needs good knives and a chopping board.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每个厨师都需要好的刀具以及案板。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>every 后再次出现，every 用 <strong>“it” 指代</strong>； every 还表 <strong>“每隔”</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Every store has a manager in charge of it.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每个商店都有管理它的经理。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Every area has its own park.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每个区域都有自己的公园</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>There are buses into town every ten minutes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每隔10分钟就有公交车发车去城里。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I leave the house every morning at 6 am.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我每天早上6点离开家。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>everyday 表 “通常的，日常的” (<strong>定语</strong>)； every day 表 “每天" (<strong>状语</strong>)。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>In the Soviet Union, poetry was at the center of everyday life.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>在苏联，诗歌是日常生活的中心。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The boys meet up every day in the park.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>everyone 表每个人</strong>； every one 指代<strong>上文提到过</strong>的名词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Everyone enjoyed themselves.</li>
<li>I received more than a hundred letters from him while i was away and I've kept every one.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我离开的时候收到100多封他的信，我留着每一封。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>every other + 名词</strong>：表 “轮流，交替，每隔…”
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We have English lessons every other day.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们每隔一天上一次英语课。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>否定代词 neither, no, none 用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>no 的用法</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>“没有”
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There are no pockets in these trousers.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这些裤子没有裤兜。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>There's no chance（=no possibility ）of us getting there by eight.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们不可能在8点之前到达那里。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表 <strong>否定答复</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Would you like any more cake？No, thank you.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你想再来点蛋糕吗？不用，谢谢。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Do you have any homework tonight？No.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你今晚有作业吗？没有。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>与形容词，副词连用，表“并不，毫不"。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The exam is no more difficult than the tests you’ve been doing in class.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这次考试并不比你们一直做的课堂测验难</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The issues are of no great interest (=only a little interest) to me.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我对这些问题不大感兴趣。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>neither 的用法</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>neither 表 <strong>两个都不</strong>，做主语时谓语动词<strong>用单数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Weve got two TVs, but neither works properly.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们有两台电视，但没有一台是好的。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Chris wasn't at the meeting and neither was her assistant.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>克里斯没有出席会议，她的助手也没有</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>“neither… nor” 结构中，表 “<strong>既不…不</strong>” 。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Neither my mother nor my father went to university.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我父母都没有上过大学。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They speak neither French nor German, but a strange mixture of the two.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们说的既不是法语也不是德语，而是两者的古怪混合。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>none 的用法</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>none 表<strong>两个以上</strong>的人或物；</li>
<li>表 “<strong>所有人都不…</strong>” 时，谓语动词<strong>多用复数</strong>；根据语境判断
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We have three sons but none of them <strong>lives/live</strong> nearby.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们有三个儿子，但是他们都不住在附近/他们没有一个住在附近。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表 “<strong>其中一个不…</strong>” 时，谓语动词<strong>多用单数</strong>。根据语境判断
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He told me all the news but none of it <strong>was</strong> very exciting.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他告诉了我全部的消息，但是没有一个是好消息。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>one 的用法</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>泛指"人们”</strong>；
<ul dir="auto">
<li>One would think the airlines would have to close down.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>人们认为航空公司将会倒闭</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The young comedian was awful； One felt embarrassed for him.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这个年轻的喜剧演员太糟糕了；人们为他感到羞愧。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>= you</strong>;
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If one fails, then one must try harder next time.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>如果你失败了，下一次你必须更努力。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>one's = his</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>One must learn from one's mistakes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>人必须从他的错误中汲取教训。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>One must be conscientious about one’s dental hygiene.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>人必须注意他的牙齿卫生。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表<strong>不确定的人或物</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>One is hardly enough.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>一个远远不够。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>One is purple, the other green.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>一个是紫色，另一个是绿色。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>one…the other : 表示 两者中的一个…另一个…</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>代替<strong>前文提过的可数名词</strong>，但并非指同一物
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Those are lovely scarves. I think I'll buy one.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这些围巾很可爱。我想买一条</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表<strong>其中之一</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's a present for one of my children.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这是我的一个孩子的礼物。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We think of you as one of the family.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们把你看做家庭的一份子。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>other, the other, others, the others, another 用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>other 的用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>作限定词</strong>后跟<strong>不可数名词</strong>或<strong>复数名词</strong>，<strong>没有复数形式</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Some music calms people； other music has the opposite effect.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>一些音乐能使人镇静，另外一些有相反的作用。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作代词</strong>， other <strong>有单复数形式</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is always ready to help others.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他总是乐于助人。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We have to solve this problem, more than any other, todday.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们今天必须优先处理这个问题。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She gave me one book last week and promised to bring the others on Wednesday.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>上周她给了我一本书，并答应周三把其他的书带来。（特指时，可用 the others）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作限定词</strong>后不可跟单数名词，如要跟，需在 other 前加 <strong>the other + 单数名词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I don' t like the red one. I prefer the other color.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我不喜欢红色的那件，我更喜欢其他的颜色</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>the other 的用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作限定词</strong>：<strong>+单数名词</strong>，表两个中的<strong>另外一个</strong>;</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作限定词</strong>：<strong>+复数名词</strong>，表群体中<strong>剩下的另一些</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This computer here is new. The other computer is about five years old.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这儿的这台电脑是新的，另外一台用了约5年了。（两台电脑）</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Where are the other two dinner plates I can only find four.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>其他两个晚饭用的盘子呢？我只找到四个。（总共六个）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作代词</strong>：指代<strong>上文提到过</strong>的人或物。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She has two kittens, one is black and the other is all white.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她有两只小猫，一只是黑色的，一只是白色的。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>another 的用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>作限定词</strong>，后 <strong>+单数名词</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Im going to have another plece of cake
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我要再吃块蛋糕。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We can fit another person in my car.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我车里还可以再坐一个人。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作代词</strong>，<strong>指代单数</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She's finished with that boyfriend and found herself another（one）.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她和原来那个男朋友分手了，又另找了一个。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Do you want to exchange this toaster for another（one ）or do you want your money back？
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你是想另换一台烤面包机，还是要退货</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>one another</strong> “<strong>互相，彼此</strong>”
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They gave one another presents when they met at the airport.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们在机场见面时互赠了礼物。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>one way or another : 用某种方法，想方设法</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We'll get out of this mess one way or another.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们得想个什么办法摆脱这种困境。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>one… after another : 一个接一个，接连</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I'm not surprised he's feeling ill — he was eating one ice cream after another！
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他生病我不觉得奇怪——他不停嘴地吃冰激凌！</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-28-互相代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#28-互相代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.8 互相代词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>相互代词只有两个</strong>：<strong>each other</strong> 和 <strong>one another</strong>，表示相互关系。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">句法作用</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>可作宾语、定语，不做主语。</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>作宾语：</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They kept looking at each other and smiling.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们一直微笑着看着对方。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The two countries went to war with one another over oil prices.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>因为油价，两国发生了战争。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作定语：</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They re always wearing each other's clothes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们总是换着衣服穿。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Apes spend a great deal of time grooming one another's.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>猴子花费大量时间互相梳理身上的皮毛</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">相互代词有时可以<strong>拆分开</strong>来使用，可<strong>做主语</strong>或主语同位语</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Each wants to know the other's income.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>彼此都想知道对方的收入</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We each know what the other want.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们知道对方要什么。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-29-疑问代词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#29-疑问代词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.9 疑问代词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">包括 what, who, whose, whom, which 引导特殊疑问句；可作<strong>主语, 宾语，表语，定语</strong>。</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Who are all those people？
那些人是谁？</li>
<li>Whom did they invite？
他们邀请了谁？</li>
<li>Whose bag is this？（定语）
这个包是谁的？</li>
<li>What caused the accident？（主语）
是什么导致了那场事故？</li>
<li>Which doctor did you see- Seward？（定语）
你看的是哪一位医生—西沃兹医生吗？</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>-ever</strong> 加在 who, which, what 后面加以<strong>强调表惊讶</strong>；表“<strong>到底，究竟</strong>"之意;</p>
<p dir="auto">相当于 no matter who/which/what</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Either Thursday or Friday – whichever day is best for you？
星期四或星期五都行—哪个日子你最方便？</li>
<li>Whoever is in charge of International Sales？
负责国际销售的人是谁？</li>
<li>Whatever is he doing with that rod？
他拿着那根竿子到底在做什么？</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026221426009.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026221426009.png" alt="image-20201026221426009" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026221557526.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026221557526.png" alt="image-20201026221557526" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-三数词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#三数词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>三、数词</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-31-基数词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#31-基数词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>3.1 基数词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>个位数词</strong>，即1-10：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>one two three four five six seven eight nine</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示**“十几”**：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>除了 11,12 为 eleven, twelve 之外，在所对应的个位数的词后加 <strong>“-teen”</strong>
9 nine — 19 nineteen</li>
<li>注意：thirteen, fiften, eighteen 的拼写。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>几十</strong>，即 20-90：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">在所对应的十位数的整数后加 <strong>“-ty”</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">12 twelve — 20 twenty</p>
<p dir="auto">13 thirteen — 30 thirty</p>
<p dir="auto">14 fourteen — 40 forty</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">注意：twenty, thirty, forty, fifty, eighty的拼写。</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>几十几</strong>，即 21-99：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">十位数词加个位数词，</p>
<p dir="auto">21— 20+1 — twenty one</p>
<p dir="auto">32— 30+2 — thirty two</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>百位数词</strong>及以上：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">100 a/one hundred</p>
<p dir="auto">1000 a/one thousand</p>
<p dir="auto">10,000 ten thousand</p>
<p dir="auto">100,000 a hundred thousand</p>
<p dir="auto">1,000,000 a million</p>
<p dir="auto">10,000,000 ten million</p>
<p dir="auto">100,000,000 a hundred million trillion 万亿</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">注意：</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>在100以上的数中， hundred 之后加 and</strong>；
<ul dir="auto">
<li>2356 two thousand three hundred and fifty six</li>
<li>1012 one thousand and twelve</li>
<li>56789 fifty six thousand seven hundred and eighty nine</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>表示整数百时， hundred 后不能加 “s”</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>two hundreds（ x）</li>
<li>two hundred （v）</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>基数词</strong>可以用来表示<strong>年龄</strong>与<strong>年代</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is his thirties.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他 30 多岁</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>1980’s.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>二十世纪八十年代</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>数字的写法&amp;念法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">百位与十位之间加 and；</p>
<p dir="auto">十万位和万位，亿位和干万位之间加 and；</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">英语大数字<strong>从右向左看</strong>，每隔<strong>三位划一逗号</strong>,</p>
<p dir="auto">倒数第一个逗号之前要用 thousand,</p>
<p dir="auto">倒数第二个逗号之前要用 million，</p>
<p dir="auto">倒数第三的逗号之前要用 billion 表示</p>
</li>
</ol>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026223607080.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201026223607080.png" alt="image-20201026223607080" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-32-序数词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#32-序数词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>3.2 序数词</h3>
<p dir="auto">表示顺序或在某个序列中所处的位置，“第几”</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示 <strong>第1~3</strong>：first, second, third，也可用1st，2nd，3rd 表示</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示 <strong>第4~19</strong>：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>fourth</th>
<th>fifth</th>
<th>sixth</th>
<th>seventh</th>
<th>eighth</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ninth</td>
<td>tenth</td>
<td>eleventh</td>
<td>twelfth</td>
<td>thirteenth</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>fourteenth</td>
<td>fifteenth</td>
<td>sixteenth</td>
<td>seventeenth</td>
<td>eighteenth</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>nineteenth</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>第几十</strong>：将相应的<strong>基数词尾的 y 变为 i + eth</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>20 twenty = 第20 twentieth</li>
<li>30 thirty = 第30 thirtieth</li>
<li>40 forty = 第40 fortieth</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>第21~99</strong>：<strong>十位数用相应的基数词</strong>，<strong>个位数用相应的序数词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>第21 twenty + frst = twenty first</li>
<li>第32 thirty + second = thirty second</li>
<li>第59 fifty + nine = fifty ninth</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>第100及以上</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>整数词</strong>：在其相应的<strong>基数词后加th</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>第100：hundredth</li>
<li>第1000：thousandth</li>
<li>第1000,000：millionth</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>非整数词</strong>：<strong>保留相应的基数词</strong>部分，但是对应的<strong>个位要用序数词</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>第1001：one thousand and first.</li>
<li>第2356：two thousand three hundred and fifty sixth.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>序数词用来<strong>表示日期</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>June 2nd, 6月2号</li>
<li>May 5th, 5月5号</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-33-数词的句法作用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#33-数词的句法作用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>3.3 数词的句法作用</h3>
<p dir="auto">数词在句中可以做主语，宾语，表语，同位语，定语以及状语。</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>做主语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Millions of people live in poverty.</li>
<li>Three of his colleagues were sacked yesterday.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作表语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There <strong>were</strong> two hundred people at the meeting.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作定语</strong>; 后面有名词修饰
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We encompassed the city with two <strong>divisions</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们用两个师包围了这座城市。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She ticked off three <strong>items</strong> on the list.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她用记号标出表格上的三个项目。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作同位语</strong>; 对 名词/代词 的解释说明
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They four tried to climb the mountain.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们四个努力爬上山顶。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We three finish the task together.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们三个完成了这项任务。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>做宾语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The children <strong>arrived in</strong> twos and threes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>孩子们三三两两地到了。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The museum <strong>was opened</strong> on 25th June 2008.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>做状语</strong>; 单独存在/修饰动词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's <strong>happened</strong> hundreds of times.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这件事发生了几百次。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>He <strong>came</strong> tenth in the new york marathon.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>纽约马拉松他得了第10名。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-四冠词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#四冠词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>四、冠词</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-41-冠词的基本含义及用法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#41-冠词的基本含义及用法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>4.1 冠词的基本含义及用法</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>冠词分为定冠词，不定冠词以及零冠词。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>After the long day, the cup of tea tasted particularly good.（定冠词）</li>
<li>After a long day, a cup of tea tastes particularly good.（不定冠词）</li>
<li>like to play basebal.（零冠词）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>定冠词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">特指</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表 “<strong>这个，那个</strong>”；替代 “this, that”;</li>
<li><strong>特指</strong> 某个名词；</li>
<li>后可 + 单数名词, 复数名词, 不可数名词。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Please give me the nail.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表 上文已提到的人或物。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The girl's eight and the boy's fourteen.</li>
</ul>
