</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">地球上具体地理位置点。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the north pole 北极</li>
<li>the equator 赤道</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">某些江河湖海</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the nile 尼罗河</li>
<li>the pacific 太平洋</li>
<li>the Yangtze River 长江</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">唯一存在的事物</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the sun太阳</li>
<li>the wind风</li>
<li>the world世界</li>
<li>the earth地球</li>
<li>the white house白宫</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">注意：如果提到上述的<strong>唯一事物的具体情况</strong>时，应使用<strong>不定冠词</strong>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I could hear the wind.</li>
<li>There's a cold wind blowing.</li>
<li>What are your plans for the future？</li>
<li>She has a promising future ahead of her.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">最高级前使用 the；</p>
<p dir="auto">表强调时使用 the</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The great Wall is the place to go.</li>
<li>You dont mean you met the Tony Blair.</li>
<li>He is the strongest among students.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">乐器前加 the</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>play the piano 弹钢琴</li>
<li>play the flute 吹长笛</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027150038495.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027150038495.png" alt="image-20201027150038495" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>定冠词 the 的用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表特指的人或事物
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The man with a flower in his hand is jack.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the man</em> 特指这个男人</li>
<li><em>with a flower in his hand</em> 介词短语充当定语，修饰名词</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>复述前面提到过的人或物
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There is a man under the tree. The man is called Robert.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>a man</em> 泛指一个人</li>
<li><em>the man</em> 特指前面提到过的人</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表独一无二的事物
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The earth turns around the sun.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the earth</em> 独一无二的事物</li>
<li><em>turns</em> 动词表现时态</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用在表示方位的名词前面
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There will be strong wind to the south of the Yangtze River.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the south</em> 方位</li>
<li>这里经常刮大风：<em>there will be</em> 改成 <em>there is</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>在序数词和形容词最高级的前面
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Who is the first one to go?
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the first</em> 序数词前</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Of all the stars , the sun is the nearest to the earth.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the stars</em> / <em>the sun</em> / <em>the earth</em> 独一无二的事物</li>
<li><em>the nearest</em> 形容词最高级前</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用在江河、海洋、山脉等名称的前面
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I have never been to the Himalaya Mountains.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the Himalaya Mountains</em> 山脉</li>
<li><em>have never been to</em> 现在完成时</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用在 含有普通名词的专有名词 的前面
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is from the United States of America.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the United States of America</em> 专有名词</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用在姓氏之前表示一家人
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The Greens are going to Mount Emei next month.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the Greens</em> 格林一家人</li>
<li><em>are going to</em> 一般将来时</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>固定短语搭配
<ul dir="auto">
<li>at the same time (与此同时) ；make the bed (铺床) ；</li>
<li>in the end (最后) ；all the time (一直)；</li>
<li>by the way (顺便说一下) ；on the way (在路上) ；</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>乐器名称前
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He began to play the violin at the age of 5.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>the violin</em> 乐器</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-42-不定冠词-aan" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#42-不定冠词-aan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>4.2 不定冠词 a/an</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>泛指人或物，后<strong>加单数可数名词</strong>。</li>
<li>第一次提到某人/物之前。</li>
<li>不与代词连用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>My shirt is dirty.（v）</li>
<li>The My shirt is dirty （x）</li>
<li>This car is expensive.（v）</li>
<li>This the car is expensⅳve.（×）</li>
<li>One person is in the reception. （v）</li>
<li>The one person is in the reception.（×）</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>和名词连用<strong>作表语或同位语</strong>，<strong>表职业</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She is a student.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她是个学生。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>am an English teacher.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我是一个英语老师。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>am a builder.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我是一个工人。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用于<strong>价格、速度、频率短语</strong>。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>sⅸ kilometers an hour
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每小时60公里</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>4 times a day
<ul dir="auto">
<li>每天四次</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>固定短语
<ul dir="auto">
<li>take a break 休息一下;</li>
<li>as a matter of fact 事实上;</li>
<li>have a good time 玩得开心;</li>
<li>in a word 总而言之;</li>
<li>make a IIving 谋生;</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027152528218.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027152528218.png" alt="image-20201027152528218" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>不定冠词 a / an 的用法</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>不定冠词 a / an 用在单数名词的前面</li>
<li>a 用在辅音开头的词前面</li>
<li>an 用在元音开头的词前面</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>具体用法：</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">泛指某一个人或物</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">There is a dog lying on the ground.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><em>There is</em> 符合主谓一致的就近原则</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><em>lying on the ground</em> 非谓语动词作定语来修饰 <em>dog</em></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><em>a</em> 泛指一只狗</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示类人或物，区别于其它种类</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>An elephant is much stronger than a man.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>元音 e 前面用 <em>an</em> ，辅音 m 前用 <em>a</em></li>
<li><em>An elephant， a man</em> 表示类别</li>
<li>比较结构 <em>much stronger than</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示“一”这个数量</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There is a table and four chairs in that dining-room.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>a table</em> 一张桌子</li>
<li><em>four chairs</em> 四把椅子</li>
<li><em>there be</em> 句型 就近原则：根据后面名词是复数则用 <em>are</em> 单数用 <em>is</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">用不定冠词的习惯用语</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">a bit (一点)	a little (一点)	a few (几个)	a lot (许多)</p>
<p dir="auto">a kind of (一种)     a pair of (一副、一双)    a number of (大量的)</p>
<p dir="auto">a piece of (一片)    half an hour (半小时)    have a good time (玩的开心)</p>
<p dir="auto">have a cold (感冒)    make a noise (发出噪音)    have/take a rest (休息一下) 等</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-43-零冠词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#43-零冠词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>4.3 零冠词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">广义的概念</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Religion is an important issue.</li>
<li>Mexican food is spicy.</li>
<li>People are worried about rising crime.</li>
<li>Information is important to any organization.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">人名，书名，剧名</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I have read Romeo and juliet.</li>
<li>Shakespeare.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">某些城镇，城市，州或国家名</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Cape Town.</li>
<li>Vietnam.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">注意：含有 state（s）， kingdom, republic, union的国名除外。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The USA, The UK, The Netherlands, The Czech Republic, The Philippines</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">某些湖泊，单独岛屿，大洲或山名</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Lake victoria</li>
<li>Jamaica</li>
<li>Asia</li>
<li>Mt Fuji</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">星球</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Mars 火星</li>
<li>Jupiter 木星</li>
<li>Saturn 土星</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">球类：棋类：语言：学科</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>例如：soccer, tennis</li>
<li>i like to play baseball.</li>
<li>My sister was always good at math.</li>
<li>i have studied french for 3 years.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">早中晚餐; 季节；日期</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>例如：breakfast, lunch, dinner, supper等</li>
<li>Let's go out for dinner tonight.</li>
<li>It' s August 28th.</li>
<li>Winter is coming.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027154618136.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027154618136.png" alt="image-20201027154618136" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>零冠词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>专有名词 和 第一次使用一些不可数名词 时前面通常不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>China is a very large country.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>China</em> 专有名词</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Man needs air and water.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>air and water</em> 第一次使用不可数名词</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>名词前已有指示、物主或不定代词 作定语修饰时不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>My pen is much more expensive than yours.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>my pen</em> 物主代词</li>
<li><em>much more expensive than</em> 比较级</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>周名、月名、日期 或 季节名前不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He was born on Monday , February 18 , 1995.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>Monday , February 18 , 1995</em>  周名/月名/日期</li>
<li><em>was born</em> 一般过去时的被动语态</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They usually plant trees in the hills in spring.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>spring</em> 季节； <em>the spring</em> 表特指不是零冠词</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>第一次使用 复数名词表示人或事物的 类别 时不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Men are cleverer than monkeys.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>特指可以加 the</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>三餐、学科前不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We have breakfast at home and lunch at school.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>and lunch</em> 省略了 <em>we have</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We all like English.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>节假日前不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>On Children's Day the boys often get presents from their parents.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>On Children's Day</em> 介词短语作时间状语</li>
<li><em>often</em> 一般现在时</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>球类前不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The children play football on Saturday afternoons.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>play football</em> 球类不用</li>
<li><em>on Saturday</em> 日期不用</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>一些习惯用语中不用（查询中文并背诵）
<ol dir="auto">
<li>at / to / from /out of / after / for school ;</li>
<li>in / to / for / after class ;</li>
<li>in / to / for /out of / into bed ;</li>
<li>after / at / from /out of /to work ;</li>
<li>at / to sea ;</li>
<li>in / from / down / to town ;</li>
<li>at / from home ;</li>
<li>at / for / to breakfast / lunch / supper ;</li>
<li>at night / noon / midnight ;</li>
<li>on foot ;</li>
<li>go to school / bed ;</li>
<li>on top of ;</li>
<li>in front of ;</li>
<li>on show / display / duty / watch ;</li>
<li>in / out of hospital ;</li>
<li>at all ;</li>
<li>on / in time ;</li>
<li>at first / last / once ;</li>
<li>in Chinese / English ;</li>
<li>take care of ;</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>序数词作副词时前面不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He came first in the race. Work must come first.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>头衔、职位、称呼前一般不用
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This is Doctor Li.</li>
<li>The guards took the American to General Lee.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027155657788.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027155657788.png" alt="image-20201027155657788" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-五形容词副词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#五形容词副词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>五、形容词、副词</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-51-形容词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#51-形容词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1 形容词</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>形容词常见形容词后缀（阅读并背诵）</li>
</ul>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>-able, -ible</th>
<th>comfortable, inevitable, incredible, invisible</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>-al, -ial</td>
<td>normal, industrial, official, beneficial</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>-ful</td>
<td>beautiful, harmful, peaceful, wonderful</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>-ic</td>
<td>economic, heroic, romantic</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>-ical</td>
<td>aeronautical, political, economical</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-511-形容词的分类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#511-形容词的分类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1.1 形容词的分类</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>属性形容词</strong>：表示人或物所具有的属性</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>active</th>
<th>主动的, 活跃的</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>adaptable</td>
<td>适应性强的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>adroit</td>
<td>灵巧的, 机敏的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>aggressive</td>
<td>有进取心的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>alert</td>
<td>机灵的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ambitious</td>
<td>有雄心壮志的</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>属性形容词前可加 “rather” 或 “very” 修饰。</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Actually, i did rather well in my exams.</li>
<li>The situation is very serious.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>类属形容词</strong>：指明事物所属的类别</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>financial</th>
<th>electric</th>
<th>classic</th>
<th>central</th>
<th>modern</th>
<th>international</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>economic</td>
<td>intellectual</td>
<td>historic</td>
<td>proper</td>
<td>legal</td>
<td>internal</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>annual</td>
<td>alternative</td>
<td>blind</td>
<td>social</td>
<td>local</td>
<td>eternal</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>domestic</td>
<td>considerable</td>
<td>ideal</td>
<td>rural</td>
<td>separate</td>
<td>empty</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>industrial</td>
<td>official</td>
<td>basic</td>
<td>traditional</td>
<td>potential</td>
<td>inevitable</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表示国籍的词属于类属形容词
<ol dir="auto">
<li>British island 英国岛屿</li>
<li>American people 美国人</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li><strong>类属形容词没有比较级与最高级</strong>，且前可<strong>不加 “rather” 或 “very“ 修饰</strong>。</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>颜色形容词</strong>：</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>blue</th>
<th>green</th>
<th>purple</th>
<th>yellow</th>
<th>red</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>pink</td>
<td>brown</td>
<td>black</td>
<td>grey</td>
<td>white</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>orange</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表示<strong>浅色</strong>可在颜色形容词前加 <strong>“light”</strong></li>
<li><strong>深色</strong>可在颜色形容词前加 <strong>”dark”</strong> 或 <strong>“deep”</strong> 另外可用 “pale, bright” 等词。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>light brown 浅褐色</li>
<li>light green 浅绿色</li>
<li>dark blue 深蓝色</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>强调形容词</strong>：强调作用</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>常见：absolute, utter, total, entire, sheer等。</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We have absolute confidence in victory.</li>
<li>This is a sheer fabrication.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>-ing&amp;-ed 形容词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">某人，某事或某个情景的性格或特点。表 “…ing, <strong>令人感觉…”</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">形容感觉或情感，表 “…ed, <strong>自己感觉…</strong>”</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is bored.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is boring.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I am confused.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I am confusing.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>常见 -ing 与 -ed 形容词（建议阅读并背诵）</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>alarmed -alarming</th>
<th>charmed -charming</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>amused -amusing</td>
<td>confused -confusing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>annoyed - annoying</td>
<td>convinced - convincing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>astonished- astonishing</td>
<td>depressed- depressing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>astounded -astounding</td>
<td>disappointed -disappointing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>challenged -challenging</td>
<td>discouraged-discouraging</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>复合形容词</strong>：两个单词构成的形容词，用连字符连接</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>复合形容词常见形式</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>形容词 + 名词 + -ed</li>
<li>形容词/副词 + 过去分词</li>
<li>形容词/副词/名词 + 现在分词</li>
<li>名词 + 形容词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is a well-known writer.</li>
<li>That was a record-breaking jump.</li>
<li>She is a world-famous singer.</li>
<li>It was a last-minute decision</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-512-形容词词序" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#512-形容词词序"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1.2 形容词词序</h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>(限定词+程度副词) + 描绘性形容词+表大小 (长短、高低形状+表状态的形容词+表年龄 (新旧) 的形容词+表颜色的形容词+表图案形容词+表国籍或产地的形容词+表物质材料的形容词+表类别或用途的形容词+名词。</li>
</ul>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>限定词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a, an, the, my your, four, those, some等。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>描绘性形容词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>beautiful, boring stupid, delicious, useful, lovely comfortable等。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>大小
<ul dir="auto">
<li>big, small, tall huge, tiny</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>形状，重量，长短
<ul dir="auto">
<li>round, square, circular, skinny fat, heavy straight, long short</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>状态
<ul dir="auto">
<li>broken, cold, hot wet, hungry, rich, easy, difficult, dirty</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>年龄
<ul dir="auto">
<li>old, young, new, ancient, antique</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>颜色
<ul dir="auto">
<li>green, white, blue, reddish purple</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>图案
<ul dir="auto">
<li>striped, spotted checked, flowery</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>国籍
<ul dir="auto">
<li>American British Italian eastern Australian Chilean</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>物质材料
<ul dir="auto">
<li>gold wooden, silk paper, synthetic, cotton woolen</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>类别或用途
<ul dir="auto">
<li>sleeping（bag）， wedding（dress）</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027165608824.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027165608824.png" alt="image-20201027165608824" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>练习
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>一个紫色漂亮的大木桌子</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a beautiful big purple wooden desk</li>
<li><strong>（限定词+描述性+大小+颜色+材质+名词）</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>个旧的漂亮的黑色的日本的方形木制小写字桌。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a pretty little square old black Japanese wooden writing desk</li>
<li>限定词+描述词1+描述词2+形状词+颜色+国籍+材质+类别+名词</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-513-句法作用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#513-句法作用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1.3 句法作用</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>作定语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It is big fat dog.</li>
<li>The car is big enough.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作表语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The news is exciting.</li>
<li>The garden is completely dry.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作补语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Money doesnt always make us happy.</li>
<li>Noises drive me crazy.</li>
<li>The was found open.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作状语</strong>: 有没有修饰名词, 没有就是状语, 表状态
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He arrived home, hungry and tired.</li>
<li>Hard to say, he is a mild boy.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>“The + 形容词”</strong> 表某一类人
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the rich</li>
<li>the poor</li>
<li>the old</li>
<li>the young</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-514-原级比较级与最高级" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#514-原级比较级与最高级"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1.4 原级、比较级与最高级</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">规则变化</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">规则</th>
<th align="center">原级</th>
<th align="center">比较级</th>
<th align="center">最高级</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center"><strong>单音节词</strong>及少数双音节词的比较级直接后加 -er，-est</td>
<td align="center">clean warm</td>
<td align="center">cleaner warmer</td>
<td align="center">cleanest warmest</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><strong>元音+辅音</strong> 字母结尾，<strong>辅音字双写</strong>后加 -er，-est</td>
<td align="center">hot big</td>
<td align="center">hotter bigger</td>
<td align="center">hottest biggest</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">不规则变化</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">原级</th>
<th align="center">比较级</th>
<th align="center">最高级</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">good/well</td>
<td align="center">better</td>
<td align="center">best</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">bad</td>
<td align="center">worse</td>
<td align="center">worst</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">many/much</td>
<td align="center">more</td>
<td align="center">most</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">little</td>
<td align="center">less</td>
<td align="center">least</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">far</td>
<td align="center">farther/further</td>
<td align="center">farthest/furthest</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">old</td>
<td align="center">older/elder</td>
<td align="center">oldest/eldest</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-515-比较级的用法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#515-比较级的用法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1.5 比较级的用法</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">单独使用，前<strong>可加修饰语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a lot, much, a little, a bit 及表数量的词。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You should be more careful.</li>
<li>The city is a lot more crowded these days.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这个城市这几天过于拥挤。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>与 than 连用</strong>, 表两者的对比</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It is more stressful than simultaneous interpreting.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>它比同声传译压力更大。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>It was much further to the town center than I remembered.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>去市中心的路比我印象中要长得多。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">其他特殊结构</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>more and more “越来越…”</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The weather is getting hotter and hotter.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>天气越来越热。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The country is becoming more and more prosperous.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这个国家越来越繁盛了</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>the more…the more + 句子(主谓)</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The longer the war lasts, the more the people suffer.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>战争持续越久，人们受难就越多。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The thicker a mammal's skin is, the less hair it has.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>哺乳动物的皮越厚，毛发越稀疏。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>more than</strong> 用法</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>more than + 名词 = not only</strong></li>
<li><strong>more than + 数词 = over</strong></li>
<li><strong>more than + 形容词 = very</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Hibernation is more than sleep.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>冬眠不仅仅是睡觉。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>More than 10 million has witnessed tremendous changes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>超过1000万人见证了巨大的变化。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They are more than happy to see us.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>见到我们，他们非常高兴。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">**more … than **</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>**比 … 多 **</li>
<li><strong>与其 … 不如…</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The book is more useful than that one.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这本书比那本书有用。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She is more a singer than an actress.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>与其说她是个演员，不如说是个歌唱家。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">no more than 与 not more than</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>no more than;</strong>      <strong>仅仅, 只有</strong></li>
<li><strong>not more than;</strong>     <strong>不超过, 不多余</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She has no more than three books.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她只有3本书。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She has not more than three books.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她至多有3本书。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">no more than 与 not more than</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>no more … than;</strong> = either … nor ; <strong>既不…也不</strong></li>
<li><strong>not more … than;</strong>  = not so … as ; <strong>不如, 不及</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is no more a musician than a painter.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他既不是音乐家，也不是作家。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She is not more diligent than he is.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她不如他勤奋。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>less than “少于”</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The interest for music had lasted for less than two years.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>对音乐的兴趣维持了不到两年。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>no less than “多达”</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We ran no less than three miles.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们跑了3英里之远。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>no less…(形容词/副词)than</strong> ; 和…一样 ;</p>
<p dir="auto">= <strong>as…(形容词/副词)as;</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">= <strong>the same as (名词);</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">= <strong>the identical with (名词);</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is no less clever than you.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他跟你一样聪明。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>not less than;</strong> 不少于</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He has not less than seven cars.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他至少有七辆车。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027221217653.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027221217653.png" alt="image-20201027221217653" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-516-最高级的用法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#516-最高级的用法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1.6 最高级的用法</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>前一般加 the</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He is the strongest student in his class.</li>
<li>What is the least expensive way of travelling in UK？</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>可单独使用</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Mary is my best friend.</li>
<li>She's the youngest musician in the piano.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">最高级前<strong>可以添加修饰语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>far, mostly, almost, by far, very, much, quite 等。
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This method is by far the least complicated.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这个方法是目前为止最简单的。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>This is quite the most irresponsible behavior i have ever seen.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这是我见过的最不负责任的行为。</li>
<li>ir-responsible : <strong>ir- 否定前缀</strong></li>
<li>im-m/p/b = 否定前缀</li>
<li>il- 否定前缀</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>at + 形容词最高级</strong> ; 表 “处于最….的状态”</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">I knew she was at her worst.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我知道她这时情绪最糟。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The game was at its peak.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>游戏正是高潮的时候。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>“a most + 形容词”</strong> 时，意为 “非常” = <strong>very</strong> = <strong>more than</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It is a most important occasion.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这是一个非常重要的时刻。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>It was a most beautiful morning.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>那是个十分美丽的早晨。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027223722915.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027223722915.png" alt="image-20201027223722915" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-517-易混淆形容词辨析阅读并背诵" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#517-易混淆形容词辨析阅读并背诵"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.1.7 易混淆形容词辨析（阅读并背诵）</h4>

<td>经典的;优秀的;一流的<br>古典的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>comprehensible <br>comprehensive</td>
<td>可理解的,易于理解的<br>全面的,综合的</td>
<td>disinterested <br>uninterested</td>

<tr>

<td>感到遗憾的<br>使人悔恨的;令人遗憾的;不幸的;可悲的</td>

<td>精神的,心灵的<br>含有酒精的</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td>活着的,作表语,作定语时后置<br>活的,现场直播的<br>活着的,作定语可前可后,可修饰人也可修饰物<br>活泼的,栩栩如生的</td>
</tr>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>We watched the live broadcast of the opera on TV.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们通过电视观看了这部歌剧的直播</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>There was a tank of live lobsters in the restaurant.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>饭馆里有一箱活龙虾</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Who is the world's greatest living architure?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>谁是现在还健在的世界上最伟大的建筑学家?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She is a lively young girl.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她是个活泼可爱的小姑娘</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027231407828.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027231407828.png" alt="image-20201027231407828" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027231449838.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027231449838.png" alt="image-20201027231449838" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-52-副词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#52-副词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.2 副词</h3>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-521-副词分类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#521-副词分类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.2.1 副词分类</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>时间副词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示时间</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>tomorrow, now, this year, next week, soon, then, yesterday, lately, recently, immediately</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I will see you tomorrow.</li>
<li>I never get up early at the weekends.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>频度副词:</strong> 表示频繁程度</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>always, sometimes, never, once a week, hourly, every day, once a month twice a year, four times a day, every other week, daily, monthly</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I always go to bed before 11 p.m.</li>
<li>I'm usually home by 6 o'clock.</li>
</ul>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027232011279.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027232011279.png" alt="image-20201027232011279" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>地点副词</strong>: 表示地点</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>here, there, everywhere, inside, outside, home, upstairs, downstairs, across, along, round, around, in out, above, below, up, down, back, forward</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>you should go upstairs and do your homework</li>
<li>The author's name was printed below the title.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>作者的名字登在标题之下.(介词)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The cars below looked like insects.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>下面的汽车像昆虫一样.(副词)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They live in that old house on the hill.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们住在山上的那间旧农舍里.(介词)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>It's very cold so put a coat on.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>天很冷,穿上一件外套吧.(副词)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>方式副词</strong>: 表明方式行为</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>carefully, slowly, loudly, suddenly, fast, well, calmly, politely, proudly, soft</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Can you move it carefully?</li>
<li>Walk slowly.</li>
<li>The boring speech finished and everyone clapped politely.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这个无聊的演讲结束了,每个人礼貌地鼓了鼓掌.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>程度副词</strong>: 表示动作的程度</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>very, extremely, rather, almost, nearly, too, fully, absolutely slightly, simply</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He was conscious that he was talking rather too much.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他意识到他说的太多了</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The bottle's nearly empty.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>疑问副词</strong>: 构成特殊疑问句</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>how, when, where, why</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>How does it work?</li>
<li>When can i see you?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>强调副词</strong>: 强调动词,形容词</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>absolutely, completely, entirely, just, perfectly, purely, quite, really, totally, utterly, really, especially, mainly, particularly, generally, largely, only</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The lecture was not particularly interesting.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这次的课不是特别有趣.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I love Rome, especially in the spring.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我喜欢罗马,尤其是春天的罗马.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>This behavior is totally unacceptable.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>完全不能接受这样的行为.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>连接副词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>how, when, where, why</strong> 引导<strong>主语从句, 宾语从句, 表语从句</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Do you remember how the kids always loved going there?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你记得孩子们是怎么样爱上去那里的吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I wonder where they will take us to.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我在想他们会带我们到哪里去.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>That's why I left so early.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这就是我为什么早早离开.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">引导并列结构</p>
<p dir="auto">then, however, consequently, therefore 等</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He drank a glass of whisky, then another and then another.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他喝了一杯威士忌,然后一杯接一杯.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We thought the figures were correct. However , we have now discovered some errors.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们认为数字是正确的,然而,我们现在发现了错误.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>关系副词</strong>: 引导定语从句</p>
<p dir="auto">when, where, why</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's one of the few countries where people drive on the left.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>它是少数人们可以左驾的国家之</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>There are times when I wonder why I do this job.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>好几次我都想为什么我要做这份工作.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The reason why he disappeared is under inspection.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他失踪的原因正在调查中.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>句子副词</strong>: 修饰整个句子</p>
<p dir="auto">apparently, actually, chiefly, chiefly, interestingly 等</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Personally, I think the show was great.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>个人来讲,我认为这个表演很不错</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Actually, I've been very busy.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>说实话,我很忙.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027234642482.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201027234642482.png" alt="image-20201027234642482" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-522-副词的构成" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#522-副词的构成"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.2.2 副词的构成</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>以 -ly 结尾的副词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">许多副词与形容词有很大的关联,译为"…地",</p>
<p dir="auto">通常 <strong>副词 = 形容词 + ly</strong>, 此类副词词量最大.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>beautiful→ beautifully</li>
<li>important→ importantly</li>
<li>apparent→ apparently</li>
<li>former→ formerly</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>以 -y 结尾</strong>的形容词变为副词, <strong>变 -y 为 i 加 -ly</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>easy→ easily</li>
<li>busy→busy</li>
<li>lucky→ luckily</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>以元音 +e 结尾</strong>的直接<strong>加 -ly</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>definite→ definitely</li>
<li>unfortunate - unfortunately</li>
<li>extreme→ extremely</li>
<li>absolute→ absolutely</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>-wards, -wise 结尾</strong>的副词</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>-wards: inwards, eastwards, upwards, downwards</li>
<li>-wise: clockwise, lengthwise, likewise</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>形容词副词同形</strong>的词</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>traight, tight, fast, hard, early, late, high, low, right, wrong, straight, long, daily, weekly, monthly, yearly</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Adam has a fast car.(形容词)</li>
<li>Adam speak<strong>s</strong> fast.(副词)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>找动词的三种形态, 动词后面是副词</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>与形容词无关的副词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>just, quite, so, soon, too, very</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>由于发音的关系, <strong>-ly 结尾的形容词不可变为副词</strong></li>
<li>friendly, manly, womanly, brotherly, sisterly, wifely, comradely husbandly, homely, worldly, early, silly, ugly</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-523-副词的用法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#523-副词的用法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.2.3 副词的用法</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">副词的位置</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">句首</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Quickly , I changed my opinion.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>很快我就改变了主意.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Suddenly , I felt afraid.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>突然间我感觉害怕</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>句尾</strong> (单个副词,建议放句尾, 两个首尾各一个)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He speaks clearly.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他说的很清楚.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She drinks quickly.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她喝的很快.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">句中</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He normally gets good marks in exams.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他通常会在考试中取得好成绩.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I put the china carefully on the table/
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我把陶器小心地放在桌子上.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">注意:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>谓语动词与宾语之间不可以加入副词.</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I put carefully the china on the table. ( x )</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>地点副词</strong>置与<strong>否定副词</strong>置于<strong>句首</strong>时, 句子<strong>要倒装</strong>, 详见"倒装句".</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">类型</th>
<th align="center">位置</th>
<th align="center">例子</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">方式副词</td>
<td align="center">1.置于句末<br>2.句子宾语过长时, 用在主语与谓语动词之间</td>
<td align="center">I read the book <strong>quickly</strong>.<br>I <strong>quickly</strong> read the book and play games.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">地点副词</td>
<td align="center">句首或句末</td>
<td align="center"><strong>Here</strong> she is.<br> <strong>Outside</strong>, where was a small garden.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">时间副词</td>
<td align="center">句首或句末</td>
<td align="center"><strong>Yesterday</strong> I met her.<br>will go to London <strong>tomorrow</strong>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">频度副词</td>
<td align="center">句首,句中,句末均可,遵守上述规则.<br>注意: always, seldom, rarely, hardly, ever never 不可用于句首.</td>
<td align="center">I <strong>usually</strong> get up late on weekends.<br> <strong>Sometimes</strong> I go by car.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">强调副词</td>
<td align="center">句中</td>
<td align="center">Fame is often <strong>simply</strong> a matter of being in the right place at the right time.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">句子副词</td>
<td align="center">单独使用,<br>句首或句末</td>
<td align="center"><strong>Frankly</strong>, I couldn 't care less what happens to him.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">副词的句法</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>作状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We could only get seats at the back.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们只能拿到后面的位置.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Walk across the road carefully!
<ul dir="auto">
<li>过马路小心点.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作表语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Do you stay home?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你待在家里吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Is Mary around?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>玛丽在附近吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作定语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The letter was sent to the above address.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>此信件已被送往上述地址.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Do you usually wear your skirts above or below the knee?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你通常穿露膝裙还是过膝裙?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作宾补</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I saw him <strong>back</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我看见他回来了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>副词的比较级与最高级</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>规则类
<ul dir="auto">
<li>quickly
<ul dir="auto">
<li>-more quickly-(the )most quickly</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>beautifully
<ul dir="auto">
<li>-more beautifully-( the )most beautifully</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>carefully
<ul dir="auto">
<li>-more carefully-( the )most carefully</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>其他类
<ul dir="auto">
<li>soon-sooner-soonest</li>
<li>fast -faster-fastest</li>
<li>late -later- latest</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>不规则类
<ul dir="auto">
<li>far-farther/further- farthest/furthest</li>
<li>well-better-best</li>
<li>little-less-least</li>
<li>much-more-most</li>
<li>badly-worse-worst</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201028145111697.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201028145111697.png" alt="image-20201028145111697" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-六介词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#六介词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>六、介词</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-61-介词的分类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#61-介词的分类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>6.1 介词的分类</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>单个介词</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>about</th>
<th>beside</th>
<th>near</th>
<th>to</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>above</td>
<td>between</td>
<td>of</td>
<td>towards</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>across</td>
<td>beyond</td>
<td>off</td>
<td>under</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>after</td>
<td>by</td>
<td>on</td>
<td>underneath</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>against</td>
<td>despite</td>
<td>like</td>
<td>unlike</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>along</td>
<td>down</td>
<td>opposite</td>
<td>until</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>among</td>
<td>during</td>
<td>out</td>
<td>up</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>around</td>
<td>except</td>

</tr>

<td>with</td>
</tr>

<td>at</td>
<td>from</td>
<td>round</td>
<td>since</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>before</td>
<td>in</td>
<td>through</td>
<td>than</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>behind</td>
<td>inside</td>
<td>beneath</td>
<td>below</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>合成介词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>within, without, onto, into, upon, out of, alongside, toward, outside,throughout</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>分词介词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>concerning, considering, following, regarding, including, excluding</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>短语介词</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>

</tr>

<td>in front of</td>
<td>on account of</td>
<td>thanks to</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td>in place of</td>

<td>up to</td>

<td></td>

<td>outside of</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
