</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-62-介词词义分类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#62-介词词义分类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>6.2 介词词义分类</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>时间的介词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>at</strong> 6 o'cock</li>
<li><strong>on</strong> February 9th</li>
<li><strong>in</strong> Spring</li>
<li><strong>in</strong> the morning</li>
<li><strong>for</strong> several months几个月</li>
<li><strong>during</strong> 1942在1942年期间</li>
<li>表示<strong>其他时间概念的介词</strong>有
<ul dir="auto">
<li>before, after, since, until, till, between, up to,from, prior to等.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>地点的介词</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">英文</th>
<th align="center">中文</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">at</td>
<td align="center">表示在小地方</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">in</td>
<td align="center">表示在大地方</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">on</td>
<td align="center">表示毗邻,接壤,在…上面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">to</td>
<td align="center">表示在…范围外</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">above, over, on</td>
<td align="center">在…上</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">below under</td>
<td align="center">在…下面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">in front of, in the front of</td>
<td align="center">在…前面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">behind</td>
<td align="center">在…的后面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">beside</td>
<td align="center">表示在…旁边</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">near</td>
<td align="center">在…旁边</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">inside</td>
<td align="center">在…里面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">outside</td>
<td align="center">在…外面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">within</td>
<td align="center">在…范围内</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">beyond</td>
<td align="center">超越…</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">against</td>
<td align="center">靠着…</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">opposite</td>
<td align="center">在…对面</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">through/via</td>
<td align="center">穿过…</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">along</td>
<td align="center">沿着…</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I was sitting <strong>at</strong> my desk.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我坐在我的书桌上.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Dublin is <strong>on</strong> the east coast of Ireland.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>都柏林位于爱尔兰东海岸线.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The apartment <strong>below</strong> is owned by a French couple.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>下面的公寓为一对法国夫妇所有.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The metro station is right <strong>beneath</strong> the airport.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>地铁站位于机场的正下方.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>方式的介词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>表示 "方式,方法" 的介词常用 by, with, through 等</li>
<li><strong>by</strong> bicycle 骑自行车</li>
<li><strong>with</strong> scissors 用剪力</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>原因的介词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>表示原因常用 for, because of, sInce</li>
<li>I wear these old trousers <strong>for</strong> painting.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我穿这些旧裤子是为了画画.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-63-介词短语的构成" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#63-介词短语的构成"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>6.3 介词短语的构成</h3>
<p dir="auto">介词是一种虚词,表示句中词与词之间的关系,在句中不充当任何成分.介词其后的成分构成介词短语,能构成介词短语的词类如下:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>介词 + 名词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>What's the reason <strong>for your unhappiness</strong>?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你为什么不开心呢?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She did some research <strong>into the causes orack pain</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她对背部疼痛的原因做了一些调查.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 代词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I saw you <strong>with her</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我看到你和她在一起.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The boy did not want to play <strong>with them</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>小男孩不愿意和他们在一起玩.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 动名词/动名词</strong> 复合结构
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Thank you <strong>for</strong> coming here.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>感谢你来到这里.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They are good <strong>at</strong> painting.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们擅长画画.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I agree <strong>with</strong> your researching there.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我同意你在这做调研.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 形容词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>from</strong> young <strong>to</strong> old
<ul dir="auto">
<li>从年轻到年老</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Her behavior is far <strong>from</strong> satisfactory.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她的行为还远远不能让人满意.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 副词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I’ve changed my mind <strong>since then</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>从那以后我改变了主意.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I was unaware of his existence <strong>until recently</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>最近我才知道有他这么个人.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 动词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Robert accused her <strong>of stealing</strong> his idea.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>罗伯特起诉她抄袭他的想法.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Getting to the final depends <strong>on winning</strong> the semi-final.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>嬴了半决赛才能去决赛.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>On arriving</strong> at the city he called up her.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>一到城里他就给她打了一个电话.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 不定式</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I had no choice <strong>but to compromise</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我别无选择只有妥协.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>It had no effect <strong>except to make</strong> him angry.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>除惹他生气外,没产生任何效果.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 从句</strong>  谓语是动词短语; 宾语从句, 定语从句
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I am worried <strong>about where</strong> she is going.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我担心她去哪了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The film <strong>at which</strong> I fell asleep was very boring.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>电影太无聊了,我睡着了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 数词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's <strong>about</strong> 6 pm.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>差不多下午6点.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Over 100</strong> people are at the meeting.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>会上有100多人.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>介词 + 介词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They've moved <strong>far into</strong> the country.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们搬到很远的乡下去了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They left the party <strong>just before</strong> us.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们走的比我们稍早一点.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-64-介词短语的句法作用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#64-介词短语的句法作用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>6.4 介词短语的句法作用</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>作定语</strong>  有被修饰的名词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a meeting <strong>in the morning</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>早晨的一个会议</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>the road <strong>to success</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>成功的道路</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作状语</strong>  没有被修饰的对象
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She lives <strong>in Beijing</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她住在北京.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They visit the wall <strong>by bike</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他们骑自行车参观了城墙.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The barbecue was canceled <strong>because of rain</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>因为下雨,烧烤被取消了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作表语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The waiter is <strong>in</strong> a good mood.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>那个服务员心情不错.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Is it <strong>in</strong> your hand?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>在你手里吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作补语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tom put some books <strong>on the table</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tom放了些书在桌上.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Dad left his wallet <strong>in a taxi</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>爸爸把钱包忘在了一辆出租车里</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>He worked <strong>as a consultant</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他的工作是一名咨询师.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作定语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's story <strong>about the pilgrim</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这是关于朝圣的故事.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The man <strong>in the house</strong> is my teacher.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>屋子里的人是我的老师.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>作同位语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>As a teacher</strong>, she is responsible for her students.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>作为一名老师,她对她的学生负责.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-65-常见介词的辨析" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#65-常见介词的辨析"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>6.5 常见介词的辨析</h3>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-66-介词的常见固定搭配" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#66-介词的常见固定搭配"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>6.6. 介词的常见固定搭配</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>表示时间 on/in/at</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">at</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>后跟<strong>具体的时刻</strong>;</li>
<li>一天中<strong>具体的时间点</strong>;</li>
<li><strong>周末</strong>以及<strong>具体的节庆</strong>.</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>at 5 o'clock</li>
<li>at midnight</li>
<li>at the weekend</li>
<li>at the New Year</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">on</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">后跟具体的时间.</p>
<p dir="auto">即<strong>某年某月某日, 星期几</strong>.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>On August 24, 2017</li>
<li>On Monday</li>
<li>On your graduation day</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">in</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>后跟<strong>年,月</strong>;</li>
<li><strong>早,中,晚;</strong></li>
<li><strong>季节.</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>in2017</li>
<li>in September</li>
<li>in the morning</li>
<li>in Spring</li>
<li>in the 21 century</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>表示地点 on/in/at</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">at</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>某个<strong>具体的位置;</strong></li>
<li><strong>工作地点或商店</strong>;</li>
<li>后加<strong>小地点</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tom lives at No 12 Woodville Road</li>
<li>He works hard at Netease</li>
<li>at bus station</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">in</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>后接<strong>大地点</strong> 或 <strong>班级</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>in London</li>
<li>What is in the wrapped box?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>包装过的盒子里是什么?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>He found it difficult to concentrate in class
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他觉得自己很难在课堂上集中注意力</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">on</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>表在某物<strong>表面上</strong></li>
<li>后加<strong>楼层</strong>.</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The office is on the 15 th floor
<ul dir="auto">
<li>办公室在15层.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>表示方位 on/in/to</strong> (易错点)</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>in: 表A在B的内部;</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>on: 表AB接壤;</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>to: 表AB不接壤.</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">in</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Chengdu lies <strong>in</strong> the southwest of China.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>成都位于中国的西南部.(成都在中国内部)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Shanxi lies <strong>to</strong> the east of Liaoning.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>山西在辽宁东边.(山西与辽宁不接壤)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Canada lies <strong>on</strong> the north of America.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>加拿大位于美国北部.(加拿大与美国接壤)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">to</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>还可表<strong>方向</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He drives the car <strong>to</strong> the south.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他开车朝着那边去.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">on</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>在<strong>左边</strong>; 在<strong>右边</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>on</strong> the left, <strong>on</strong> the right</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>in front of / in the front of</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>in front of: 表在某物<strong>范围外</strong>的前面;</li>
<li>in the front of: 表在某物<strong>范围内</strong>的前面.</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There is a tall tree <strong>in front of</strong> the house.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>房子前面有一棵大树.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We sit <strong>in the front of</strong> the bus.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们坐在公共汽车的前部.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>in / into</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">in 静态概念</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>in: <strong>表在里面</strong>/内部;</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She' s gone for a walk in the garden.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她在花园里散步.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>She walked into the garden.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她走进了花园.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">into 动态</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>into: 常与动词连用, <strong>表动作</strong>朝着里面去.</li>
<li>有些动词两个介词均可 put, fall, jump,dive</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Can you <strong>put</strong> the milk <strong>in/into</strong> the fridge?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你能把牛奶放进冰箱吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>on / onto</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">on / upon : 表示<strong>在某物的表面上</strong>; 静态</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Your keys are on the table.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你的钥匙在桌子上</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The cat climbed onto the roof.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>猫爬上了屋顶</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">onto : 通常与动词连用, 表动作<strong>朝着…之上</strong>; 动态</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The hotel is on the road opposite the beach.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>酒店的海滩对面的路上.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The path leads onto the main road.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这条路一直到主路上.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>在河流, 道路</strong>等之上时用 on;</p>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>沿着河流, 道路</strong>朝着某个方冋时用 onto.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>below / under / beneath</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">均表 "在…之下"</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>under 表示<strong>在…之下</strong>, below 表示某物<strong>低于某物</strong>;
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The metro station is right beneath the airport.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>地铁站就在机场下面.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>His shoes were under his bed.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他的鞋在他的床下.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>There was a big clock below the painting.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>画下面有一口大钟.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表示某物<strong>接触或覆盖</strong>某物时, 用 <strong>under</strong> 不用 below;
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Under a white coat, she wore an amazing red dress. (v)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Below a white coat, she wore an amazing red dress. (x)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表<strong>时间, 重量</strong>时, 用 <strong>under</strong>; 表<strong>温度</strong>高低时, 用 <strong>below</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We finished the proje ct in <strong>under a year</strong>.(√)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We finished the project in below a year. ( x)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The roof of the new building is just <strong>below the height</strong> of the schoo.(v)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The roof of the new building is just under the height of the scnool.(x)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>below, under 后可加数字, beneath 不可加.</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We buy it for just <strong>under 300</strong> pounds. (v)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We buy it for just beneath 300 pounds.(x)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The temperature was <strong>below 10</strong> on that day. (V)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The temperature was beneath 10 on that day. (x)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表能力, 地位, 期望低时, <strong>用 beneath; 抽象概念</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The job is <strong>beneath</strong> my expectations.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201029220616298.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201029220616298.png" alt="image-20201029220616298" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-七动词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#七动词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>七、动词</h2>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420225946839.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420225946839.png" alt="image-20210420225946839" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420230308625.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420230308625.png" alt="image-20210420230308625" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-71-动词的分类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#71-动词的分类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.1 动词的分类</h3>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-711-实义动词-行为动词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#711-实义动词-行为动词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.1.1 实义动词 (行为动词)</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>用来表示动作</li>
<li>分及物动词与不及物动词
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Cats meow loudly.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>猫叫的很大声.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Students learn new material.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>学生们学习新的材料.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>及物动词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>bring, send, owe, contain, buy, show, take, tell, verify, check, get, wash, finalize, annoy, lay, lend, offer, edit, make, phone 等词<strong>后面必须跟宾语</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>His constant joking <strong>was beginning</strong> to annoy her.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他不停的嘲笑渐渐惹恼了她.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>He <strong>offered</strong> some useful advice.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他提供了一些有用的建议.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>不及物动词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>come, explode, laugh, sit, rise,excel, respond, run, cough, swim, emigrate, smile, act, cry, immigrate, lie arrive, continue, die, go 只能充当不及物动词.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If she <strong>continues</strong> to be late for work the boss will fire her.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>如果她继续迟到,老板就会开除她.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The bomb <strong>exploded</strong> in the city center.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>炸弹在市中心爆炸.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>及物动词&amp;不及物动词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>很多词既能充当及物动词,也能充当不及物动词.
set, leave, give, study, sit, grow, smell, dance, sing, write, teach burn, eat, paint, drive, manage, stop, climb, run, check, cost, go, pay, Improve 等.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The actress <strong>wiped</strong> the tears from her eyes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>女演员把眼泪从眼中擦掉.(有宾语)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The windshield wipers <strong>wiped</strong> across the windshield.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>风挡刮水器在挡风玻璃上刮来刮去.(无宾语)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-712-助动词auxiliary-verbs和情态动词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#712-助动词auxiliary-verbs和情态动词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.1.2 助动词（Auxiliary Verbs）和情态动词</h4>
<p dir="auto">①协助主要动词构成谓语的词叫助动词;
②<strong>没有实际意义, 不可单独使用</strong>
③<strong>构成时态, 语态, 否定句, 强调句, 疑问句</strong>
④主要有: have/do/be</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">基本助动词</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>be 动词</strong> 构成<strong>进行时</strong> &amp; <strong>被动语态</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">He <strong>is</strong> always <strong>spilling</strong> things.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他总是洒东西.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">This sentence <strong>was</strong> <strong>written</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这个句子被写.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">be 动词作<strong>系动词</strong>, 引表语 &amp; 表语从句</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He <strong>is</strong> in horrible pain.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他很痛.</li>
<li>China <strong>is</strong> not no longer what it used to be.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>中国不再是过去的样子.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li>have <strong>现在完成时</strong> / <strong>完成进行时</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">I <strong>have</strong> read many, many books.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我已经读了很多很多的书.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Jerry <strong>has</strong> bought a new shirt.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>杰瑞买了一件新衬衫.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">have 作实义动词, 意为"有";
有时, have 与 eat, drink 意义相同.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He <strong>has a large coffee</strong> stain on his shirt.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他的衬衫上有一大片咖啡渍.</li>
<li>Let's <strong>have a cup</strong> of tea.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们喝杯茶.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">do <strong>疑问句</strong> &amp; <strong>否定句</strong> &amp; <strong>强调句</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">He <strong>didn't</strong> put his coffee in a cup with a lid.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">他没把咖啡倒进有盖的杯子里.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Why <strong>did</strong> you do that?</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你为什么那么做?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Do</strong> come with us.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>请一定要和我们一起去.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">do作实义动词 "做,干"</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We will <strong>do</strong> what we can to help.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们会做我们能做的事情来帮忙.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>情态动词</strong>: 有含义, 和<strong>动词原形</strong>一起构成谓语.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>can / could</strong> 表"推测" "允许" "能力;
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I <strong>could</strong> fly via Amsterdam if I leave the day before.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>如果我昨天能出发的话, 我可以飞过阿姆斯特丹</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>You <strong>could</strong> take the tour of the castle tomorrow.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你可以带明天城堡的团.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>may / might</strong> 表"推测" "允许" "请求" "祝愿;
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You <strong>may</strong> start your exam now.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你现在可以开始答题了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We'd better phone tomorrow; they <strong>might</strong> be eating their dinner now.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们最好明天打电话,他们现在可能在吃晚饭.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>must</strong> 表"命令" "肯定推测";
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You <strong>must</strong> have a passport to cross the border.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你必须有护照才能通过边境.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>should/shall/ought to</strong> 表"义务,要求" "推测" "征求意见";
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Shall</strong> I help you with your luggage?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我可以帮你提行李吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I think we <strong>should</strong> check everything again.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我认为我们应该再检查一遍所有的东西.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>You <strong>ought to</strong> have your car serviced before the winter.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你应该在冬天之前保养你的车.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>would/will</strong> 表"意愿" "请求";
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>I'll</strong> do that for you if you like.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>如果你喜欢,我可以为你做.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Would</strong> you mind if I brought a colleage ith me?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你介意我带一位同事和我一起吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Would</strong> you prefer tea or coffee? "-"I'd like tea please
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"你想要茶还是咖啡"?—"茶."</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>When I was a child, I <strong>would</strong> spend hours playing with my train set.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我小的时候, 我经常花大量的时间玩玩具火车.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201030012956672.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201030012956672.png" alt="image-20201030012956672" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-713-静态动词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#713-静态动词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.1.3 静态动词</h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示思想的词</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>believe, doubt, know, understand</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示拥有的词</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>have, own,want, contain</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示感觉的词</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>hear,see, smell</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示情感的词</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ove, hate, want, need
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I like ice cream.</li>
<li>I know a lot of English words.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我知道很多英语词汇.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I hear music coming from his apartment.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我听到音乐从他的公寓传来.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>He has a Mercedes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他有一辆奔驰.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">其他<strong>常见静态动词(填写中文含义且阅读并背诵)</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>

</tr>

</tr>

</table>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-714-动词短语" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#714-动词短语"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.1.4 动词短语</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>构成:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>动词 + 介词</strong> 或 <strong>动词+副词</strong>;</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>通常<strong>与原动词含义不同</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Be sure to put on a life jacket before getting into the boat.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>坐船之前请确定穿上了救生衣.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I'm having some trouble working out the solution to this equation.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我在找这个等式的解决方法上陷入了困难.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>We're going to have to put off our vacation until next year.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我们得把假期推到明年.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Take off your shoes before you walk on the carpet.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你走到地毯上之前脱掉鞋子.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-72-动词的形式" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#72-动词的形式"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.2 动词的形式</h3>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-721-动词原形" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#721-动词原形"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.2.1 动词原形</h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>do,have,make,work等</li>
</ul>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-722-动词的第三人称单数" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#722-动词的第三人称单数"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.2.2 动词的第三人称单数</h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①一般现在时中
②主语为第三人称单数;
③谓语动词要用第三人称单数形式.</li>
</ul>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>直接动词<strong>词尾加 -s</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ask---asks
work---works
get---gets
stay---stays</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>以字母 <strong>s, x, ch, sh或 o 结尾的动词, 词尾加 -es</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>watch-watches
wish---wishes
fix— fixes
do---does
go-goes
pass---passes</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>辅音字母 -y, 变 y 为  i 加 -es;</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>try-tries
study -studiestry-tries
study -studies</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>不规则变化</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>be - am, is, are
have- has</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-723-动名词与现在分词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#723-动名词与现在分词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.2.3 动名词与现在分词</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>直接<strong>词尾加 ing</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>play-playing
cry-crying
bark-barking</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>词尾为 -e, 去掉 e 加 ing</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>slide-sliding
ride -riding</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>词尾为 ie, 变 e 为 y 加 ing</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>die-dying
tie-tying</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>辅音+元音+辅音, 双写词尾加 ing</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>beg-begging
begin-beginning</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-724-过去式与过去分词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#724-过去式与过去分词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.2.4 过去式与过去分词</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">①规则动词的过去式加"ed
②以e结尾的动词的词尾直接加"-d</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>play→ played
listen→ listened
love→ loved</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>

<td align="center">sting</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>

</table>

</tr>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">三大变形金刚</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>名词/代词: (单复数; 主格/ 宾格/ 属格/ 反身代词)</li>
<li>形容词/副词: (比较级/ 最高级)</li>
<li>动词: (单三/ <strong>现在分词</strong>/ 过去分词/ <strong>动名词</strong>/ 过去式)</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-73-动词的语法---时态" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#73-动词的语法---时态"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.3 动词的语法 - 时态</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center"></th>
<th align="center">现在时</th>
<th align="center">过去时</th>
<th align="center">将来时</th>
<th align="center">过去将来时</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">一般</td>
<td align="center">ask/asks</td>
<td align="center">asked</td>
<td align="center">shall/will ask</td>
<td align="center">should/ would ask</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">进行</td>
<td align="center">am/is/ are asking</td>
<td align="center">was/were asking</td>
<td align="center">shall /will be asking</td>
<td align="center">should/would be asking</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">完成</td>
<td align="center">have/has asked</td>
<td align="center">had asked</td>
<td align="center">shall/will have asked</td>
<td align="center">should/would have asked</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">完成进行</td>
<td align="center">have/has been asking</td>
<td align="center">had been asking</td>
<td align="center">shall/will have been asking</td>
<td align="center">should/ would have been asking</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201030150227367.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201030150227367.png" alt="image-20201030150227367" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-731-一般现在时" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#731-一般现在时"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.3.1 一般现在时</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>形式
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①肯定形式: <strong>第三人称单数</strong>的 "三单变化"; 其他用<strong>动词的原形</strong></li>
<li>②否定形式: 主语 + <strong>do/does + not</strong> + 谓语<strong>动词原形</strong></li>
<li>③疑问形式: 疑问词 + <strong>do/does</strong> + 主语 + 谓语<strong>动词原形</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用法
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>现在</strong>时段发生的动作.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I <strong>feel</strong> great!</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>习惯性动作</strong>&amp;常发生的动作.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I never <strong>drink</strong> coffee before 12.00.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>部分否定 : 肯定一部分, 否定一部分; all / both / every + not</li>
<li>全部否定 : 否定, 肯定谓语动词+否定意义的单词</li>
<li>双重否定 : 否定 + 否定</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Every monday and thursday I <strong>go</strong> to the gym.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>表示<strong>客观真理</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The earth <strong>goes</strong> round the sun.</li>
<li>Water <strong>is</strong> liquid at room temperature.</li>
<li>Gold <strong>isn't</strong> liquid at room temperature.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用于<strong>电影, 赛事, 时间的评论, 独白, 报道</strong>等.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The picture <strong>shows</strong> us how they built the road last year.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>谈论<strong>时间表,日程表</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The train <strong>leaves</strong> at half past four</li>
<li>The course <strong>starts</strong> on 1 July</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>一般现在时表将来</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>当主句为将来时态或表将来意义时,时间和条件的状语从句必须用一般现在时表将来</li>
<li>I'Il write to her when I <strong>have</strong> time.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>主将从现</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-732--一般过去时" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#732--一般过去时"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.3.2  一般过去时</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>形式
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①肯定形式: <strong>主语 + 动词过去式</strong>
②否定形式: <strong>主语 + did not + 动词原形</strong>
③疑问形式: <strong>疑问词 + did + 主语 + 动词原形</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I <strong>lived</strong> in London ten years ago.</li>
<li>We <strong>didn't</strong> like the film.</li>
<li>Where <strong>did</strong> they meet richard?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用法
<ul dir="auto">
<li>表过去发生的动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Last night I <strong>played</strong> my guitar loudly and the neighbors <strong>complained</strong>.</li>
<li>They <strong>didn't</strong> study so they <strong>didn't</strong> pass the test.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-733--一般将来时" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#733--一般将来时"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.3.3  一般将来时</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>形式
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①肯定形式:主语+ will + <strong>动词原形</strong>
②否定形式:主语+ won't(will not) + <strong>动词原形</strong>
③疑问形式:疑问词+ Will + 主语 + <strong>动词原形</strong></li>
<li>They <strong>won' t see</strong> Jane when she comes back from India</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用法
<ul dir="auto">
<li>表还没发生,未来发生的行为,动作,事件
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We <strong>won't</strong> meet them at the station</li>
<li>I <strong>will</strong> learn a new language</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>其它表将要发生
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>be going to</strong></li>
<li><strong>be to do</strong></li>
<li><strong>be about to do</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-734-现在进行时" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#734-现在进行时"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.3.4 现在进行时</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>形式
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①肯定形式:主语+ be动词 +<strong>动词ing</strong>
②否定形式:主语+ be动+not +<strong>动词ing</strong>
③疑问形式:疑问词+ be动词 +主语 +<strong>动词ing</strong></li>
<li>You <strong>are cooking</strong>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用法
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①说话的时刻正在发生的动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>I'm watching</strong> a film on TV now.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>②<strong>常与 always, constantly, continually, forever, repeatedly等词连用</strong>; 含有<strong>抱怨语气</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Her husband <strong>is always complaining</strong> about his health.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她老公总是抱怨他的健康.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>③<strong>现在进行时表示将来, 多用于已经安排好的事情</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>My son <strong>is taking</strong> his girlfriend to dinner <strong>tonight</strong>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>④ <strong>be going to</strong> 很快就要发生
<ul dir="auto">
<li>计划, 安排的动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>We <strong>are going to</strong> sing at the party</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>确定将来会发生的事情
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Look at that car it <strong>is going to</strong> crash into the yellow one</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>注意
有些动词<strong>不能用于现在进行时</strong>, 用一般现在时
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>情感类</strong>: love, hate, prefer</li>
<li><strong>所属类</strong>: have, own, want, belong</li>
<li><strong>感官类</strong>: see, hear, smell, seem</li>
<li><strong>思想类</strong>: know, believe, remember</li>
<li><strong>测量类</strong>: contain, consist, fit</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-734-现在完成时" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#734-现在完成时"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.3.4 现在完成时</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">现在完成时</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①肯定形式:主语+ have/has +<strong>过去分词</strong></li>
<li>②否定形式:主语+ haven' t(have not) hasnt( has not) +<strong>过去分词</strong></li>
<li>③疑问形式:疑问词+ have/has +<strong>过去分词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They <strong>have finished</strong> the letter.</li>
<li><strong>Has</strong> he/she <strong>finished</strong> the letter.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">用法</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">①表<strong>过去完成</strong>的动作;</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>这个动作对现在造成影响或与现在有关</li>
<li>常与 <strong>still, yet, already, always</strong>连用.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Has</strong> he <strong>repaired</strong> the lawn-mower yet?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>你修除草机了吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">②讨论<strong>个人的经历</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I <strong>haven 't seen</strong> her this month.</li>
<li><strong>I've</strong> already <strong>moved</strong> house twice this year.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">过去已经开始的动作<strong>一直延续到现在</strong>,;</p>
<p dir="auto">甚至有<strong>可能继续延续</strong>下去;</p>
<p dir="auto">常与 <strong>before, since, for, already, many times, so far,yet</strong>连用.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He has driven a car since 2002</li>
<li>They've sold 110 so far.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>到目前为止他们已经卖了110</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-734-过去完成时" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#734-过去完成时"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.3.4 过去完成时</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>形式
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①肯定形式:主语+<strong>had+过去分词</strong>
②否定形式:主语+ <strong>hadn't( had not)+过去分词</strong>
③疑问形式:疑问词+had+主语+<strong>过去分词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>They <strong>had</strong> already <strong>met</strong> Sarah before the party.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>在聚会前,他们早己见过萨拉.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I <strong>hadn't met</strong> Sarah before the party.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>在聚会前,我没见过萨拉.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Had</strong> he <strong>met</strong> Sarah before the party?
<ul dir="auto">
<li>聚会前他见过萨拉吗?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>用法
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①表过去的某个动作之前发生的动作
<ul dir="auto">
<li>She said she <strong>had</strong> <strong>written</strong> three letters the day before.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>她说那天之前她已经写了3封信.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>They <strong>had</strong> <strong>lived</strong> in york before they moved to Liverpool.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>在他们搬去利物浦之前,他们住在纽约.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>②与 <strong>after, as soon as, the moment that, unti</strong> 连用.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>After she <strong>had moved</strong> out , I found her notes.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他搬出去之后,我找了她的笔记.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I didn't say anything until she <strong>had finished</strong> talking.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>知道她说完了之后我才讲了一些.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>③与 <strong>before,when, by the time</strong>连用.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Before I knew it, she <strong>had</strong> <strong>run</strong> out the door
<ul dir="auto">
<li>我知道之前,她已经跑出了家门.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>I washed the floor when the painter <strong>had</strong> <strong>gone</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>画家离开之后我才拖了地.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>By the time he phoned her, she <strong>had</strong> <strong>found</strong> someone new
<ul dir="auto">
<li>他给她电话之时,她已经有了新的人选.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-74-动词时态---语态" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#74-动词时态---语态"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.4 动词时态 - 语态</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">定义</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>主语是动作的执行者</strong>(即某人做某事), 叫<strong>主动语态</strong>;
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Monkeys</strong> adore bananas.
猴子喜欢香蕉.</li>
<li>The <strong>dog</strong> chased the squirrel.
狗追松鼠.</li>
<li><strong>She</strong> said she had written three letters the day before.</li>
<li><strong>They</strong> had lived in York before they moved to Liverpool.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>主语是动作的承受者</strong>(即某事被做), 叫<strong>被动语态</strong>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>After the earthquake, <strong>aid</strong> was sent to the people of Haiti.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>地震后,救援被送到了海地人民手里.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <strong>electricity</strong> was cut off because the bill hadn’t been paid.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>因为没缴费,所以电被切断了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Whales</strong> must be protected by an international ban on whaling.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>鲸鱼应该受到国家禁止扑杀鲸鱼的保护.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>主动改被动步骤</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①将主动语态的<strong>宾语</strong>改为被动语态的<strong>主语</strong>;
②将主动语态的谓语动词改为 ”<strong>be+过去分词结构</strong>”;
③将主动语态的<strong>主语</strong>改为介词<strong>by之后的宾语</strong>, 放在谓语动词之后(有时可省略).</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>He</strong> gave the <strong>book</strong> to me.
The <strong>book</strong> was given to me <strong>by him</strong>.</li>
<li><strong>Someone</strong> broke into the <strong>pet shop</strong>.
The <strong>pet shop</strong> was broken into. 省略未知人物</li>
<li>They looked for the <strong>baby</strong>.
The <strong>baby</strong> was looked for.</li>
<li>Someone shouts at the man.
The man is shouted at.</li>
<li>They listen to the music.
Music is listened to.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">各个时态的被动语态</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">时态</th>
<th align="center">助动词+过去分词</th>
<th align="center">举例</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">一般现在时</td>
<td align="center">am, is, are+made</td>
<td align="center">Wine is made.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">现在进行时</td>
<td align="center">am, is, are+being+sent</td>
<td align="center">The document is being sent.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">一般过去式</td>
<td align="center">was, were+invited</td>
<td align="center">I was invited.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">过去进行时</td>
<td align="center">was, were+<br>being +washed</td>
<td align="center">Their cars were being washed.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">一般将来时</td>
<td align="center">will be +signed<br>am, is, are+<br>going to be+built</td>
<td align="center">The contract will be signed.<br>The houses are going to be built.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">现在完成时</td>
<td align="center">has, have+been+sold</td>
<td align="center">The business has been sold</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">过去完成时</td>
<td align="center">had+been+hired</td>
<td align="center">The new manager had been hired</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">将来完成时</td>
<td align="center">will+have been+finished</td>
<td align="center">The car will have been loaded</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">情态动词 can/should must</td>
<td align="center">情态动词+be+ issued</td>
<td align="center">a passport can only be issued</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">have to</td>
<td align="center">have to, has to<br>had to+be+arranged</td>
<td align="center">His party has to be arranged<br>His plans have to be arranged</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>补充1:</strong> <strong>双宾的被动语态</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>把<strong>间接宾语</strong>改为被动语态的<strong>主语</strong>, 直接宾语仍保留原位;</li>
<li>把<strong>直接宾语</strong>改为被动语态的<strong>主语</strong>, <strong>间接宾语</strong>前要加介词 <strong>to 或 for</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>His teacher gave him a dictionary.</strong>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>He</strong> was given a <strong>dictionary</strong> by his teacher.</li>
<li>a <strong>dictionary</strong> was given to <strong>him</strong> by his teacher.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>补充2:</strong> <strong>宾补的被动语态</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>主动语态的宾语改为主语,宾补在被动语态中做主语补足语.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I paint the house white.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The house is painted white by me.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>补充3:</strong> <strong>加to</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>不带 to 的动词</strong>不定式作宾补的主动语态, 被动语态时不定式要 加to</li>
<li><strong>感官动词</strong> 和 <strong>使役动词</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>The boss</strong> made the poor man work 12 hours a day.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>The poor man</strong> was made <strong>to</strong> work 12 hours a day.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>补充4: 动词短语作谓语</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>短语动词</strong>改被动语态时要保持其<strong>完整性</strong>, <strong>介词或副词</strong>不可遗漏.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The girl <strong>takes good care of</strong> her little brother.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The girls little brother is <strong>taken good care of</strong> by her</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-75-动词语法---非谓语动词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#75-动词语法---非谓语动词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.5 动词语法 - 非谓语动词</h3>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420230031839.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/%E7%8E%8B%E8%8F%B2%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95.assets/image-20210420230031839.png" alt="image-20210420230031839" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">**非谓语动词 "4有1不" **</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>非谓语动词有语态和时态的变化</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>现在式</strong>与谓语动词表示的动作同时发生.</li>
<li><strong>完成式</strong>表示的动作发生在谓语动词表示的动作之前.</li>
<li><strong>进行式</strong>与谓语动词表示的动作同时发生,表示动作正在进行.</li>
<li><strong>完成进行时</strong>表示的动作发生在谓语动词表示的动作之前,且动作持续.</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-751-动名词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#751-动名词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.5.1 动名词</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">形式</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>①动名词与现在分词同形(ving);
②起到名词的作用.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">用法</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">主语</p>
<p dir="auto">谓语动词为<strong>单数</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Jogging</strong> is a hobby of mine
慢跑是我的爱好.
<strong>Reading</strong> helps you learn English
阅读帮你学习英语.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">宾语</p>
<p dir="auto">①有的动词<strong>直接加动名词</strong>做其宾语;
②有的<strong>加介词后加动名词</strong>作其宾语.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">He quit <strong>smoking</strong> a year ago
他一年前戒烟了.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">I look forward to <strong>helping</strong> you paint the house
我期待帮你刷房子.</p>
<p dir="auto">注意:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>it+形容词+动名词</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>It</strong> is <strong>no use telling</strong> him not to worry.
告诉他别担心没有用.(i作形式主语)</p>
<p dir="auto">此类动词还包括:</p>
<p dir="auto">better, wonderful, enjoyable, interesting, foolish, difficult, useless, senseless, worthwhile</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表语</p>
<p dir="auto">对主语进一步说明, <strong>相当于一个名词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>My job <strong>is teaching.</strong>
我的工作是教书.
Seeing <strong>is believing.</strong>
眼见为实.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">定语</p>
<p dir="auto">表示用途或性质.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a swimming pool = a pool for swimming 游泳池
a moving truck 搬家汽车 = a truck for moving
drinking water饮用水
swimming suit游泳衣
sleeping pil安眠药
writing paper信纸
operating table手术室
reading room阅览室
washing machine洗衣机
washing powder洗衣粉
fishing pole钓鱼杆</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">以下动词及句型后常跟动名词作宾语(查明词义并背诵)</p>
<table>

</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-752-分词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#752-分词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.5.2 分词</h4>
<p dir="auto">①<strong>现在分词</strong>的形式同动名词一样, 在动词后面<strong>加 -ing</strong>.
②<strong>过去分词</strong>的形式则在动词后面<strong>加 -ed</strong>.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>现在分词</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">a) 现在分词为动词的 ing 形式;</p>
<p dir="auto">b) 有<strong>时态</strong>和<strong>语态</strong>的变化;</p>
<p dir="auto">c) 在句中<strong>相当于一个动词</strong>;</p>
<p dir="auto">d) 在句中可做<strong>定,状或表</strong>.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">形式</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">现在分词</th>
<th align="center">主动</th>
<th align="center">被动</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">一般式</td>
<td align="center">writing</td>
<td align="center">being written</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">完成式</td>
<td align="center">having written</td>
<td align="center">having been written</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>一般式</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">表示的<strong>动作与主语动作同时发生</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tom came <strong>sauntering</strong> up the path.
汤姆来了,在路上闲逛.</li>
<li><strong>Reaching</strong> for the flower, I lost my balance.
靠近花朵,我失去了平衡.</li>
<li>Not <strong>being able to</strong> win the game, I lost my confidence.
没能赢得比赛, 我失去了信心.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>完成式</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">表示该<strong>动作发生</strong>在<strong>谓语动词之前</strong>且<strong>已经完成</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Having heard</strong> the news, he quickly sold his brothers record collection.
听完这个消息, 他迅速卖了他哥哥收集的磁带.</li>
<li>Not <strong>having finished</strong> his work, he could not leave the office.
还没有完成工作, 所以他不能离开办公室.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">句法作用</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作定语</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">可置于名词之前做<strong>前置定语</strong>;</p>
<p dir="auto">也可<strong>构成短语</strong>置于名词之后做<strong>后置定语</strong>;</p>
<p dir="auto">相当于一个<strong>定语从句</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The man <strong>carrying</strong> the bricks (=who carrying the bricks) is my father.
扛砖的男人是我的父亲.</li>
<li>The old woman, <strong>thinking</strong> all was safe, (=who thinks all was safe.)
attempted to cross the road
认为完全安全的老妇人试图穿过马路</li>
<li>There is someone <strong>knocking</strong> at the door. (someone who is knocking)
有人在敲门.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作表语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">The news is <strong>encouraging</strong>.
这消息令人鼓舞.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The present situation is <strong>terrifying</strong>.
目前形势令人惊恐.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">My job is really <strong>tiring</strong>. I don' t get home until 10 pm sometimes.
我的工作太累了.有时晚上10点才到家.</p>
<p dir="auto">注意: 现在分词做表语<strong>相当于一个形容词</strong>, 表示主语的特征, 此类词还包括</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>amusing</strong>, charming, discouraging, exciting, interesting, inviting</p>
<p dir="auto">missing, amazing, shocking, surprising amusing, charming,</p>
<p dir="auto">discouraging, exciting, interesting, inviting, missing, amazing,</p>
<p dir="auto">shocking, surprising</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作状语</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>谓语动词</strong>发生的<strong>时间、方式、伴随、让步</strong>等, 相当于<strong>状语从句</strong>,</p>
<p dir="auto">现在分词作状语时的<strong>逻辑主语</strong>就是<strong>句子的主语</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>原因状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>He</strong> was talking to her friend and forgot everything around her.
=Talking to her friend <strong>he</strong> forgot everything around her.
由于和她的朋友聊天,所以他忘记了所有的事情.</li>
<li><strong>Since</strong> we watch the news every day we know what’s going on in the world.
=<strong>Watching the news</strong> every day we know what’s going on in the world.
因为我们每天都看新闻,所以我们知道世界上发生了什么.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>伴随状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The dog <strong>wagged</strong> its tail and <strong>bit</strong> the postman.
-<strong>Wagging</strong> its tail the dog <strong>bit</strong> the postman.
狗摇着尾巴,咬了邮递员.</li>
<li>The man was <strong>sitting</strong> in the cafe. He was <strong>reading</strong> a paper.
=The man was <strong>sitting</strong> in the cafe <strong>reading</strong> a paper.
那个男人坐在咖啡店,读报纸.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>**时间状语 **= 时间状语从句
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>While</strong> she was tidying up her room she found some old photos.
=<strong>Tidying up</strong> her room <strong>she found</strong> some old photos.
整理房间时,她发现了一些旧照片.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>条件状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If they do not have enough money they will spend their holidays at home next year.
=<strong>Not having enough money</strong> they will spend their holidays at home next
year.
如果没有足够的钱,他们明年就在家度过假期.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>结果状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Carbon burns in oxygen or air, thereby <strong>forms</strong> carbon dioxide.
=Carbon burns in oxygen or air, thereby <strong>forming</strong> carbon dioxide.
碳在氧气中燃烧,形成二氧化碳.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>过去分词</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">句法作用</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作表语</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">表示谓语动词所处的状态.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I was <strong>alarmed</strong> by the loud bang.
听到巨大的响声,我受到了惊吓.</li>
<li>He was <strong>amused</strong> to hear his little son singing in the bath.
听到他的小儿子在浴室里低声唱歌,他被逗笑了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作定语</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①过去分词做可以置于名词之前做前置定语, 也可以构成短语置于名词之后做后置定
语.</p>
<p dir="auto">②过去分词作定语相当于一个<strong>定语从句</strong>, 与其逻辑主语构成<strong>被动关系,</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A <strong>burnt</strong> child (=a child who <strong>is burnt</strong> ) dreads fire.
烧伤的男孩害怕火.</li>
<li>The musicians stood up, <strong>surrounded</strong> by thunderous applause. (=who <strong>is</strong>
<strong>surrounded</strong> by thunderous applause.)
音乐家们站起来,受到雷鸣般的掌声.</li>
<li>This is the last photograph <strong>taken of</strong> my grandmother. (which <strong>is taken of</strong> my
grandmother.)
这是最后一张给奶奶照的照片.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>做状语</strong>, 和过去分词相同</p>
<p dir="auto">过去作状语表示谓语动词发生的<strong>时间, 方式, 伴随, 让步</strong>等,</p>
<p dir="auto">相当于一个<strong>状语从句</strong>,</p>
<p dir="auto">过去分词作状语时的<strong>逻辑主语</strong>就是句子的主语.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>原因状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Battered</strong> by the wind, John fell to his knees.
<strong>=Because</strong> he <strong>was battered</strong> by the wind, John fell to his knees.
由于受到大风猛吹,约翰跪倒在地.</li>
<li><strong>Deceived</strong> by his friends, he committed suicide.
=since he <strong>was deceived</strong> by his friends, he committed suicide.
受到朋友欺骗,他自杀了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>时间状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Seen from</strong> the hill, the town looks magnificent.
=when it <strong>is seen</strong> from hill, the town looks magnificent.
从山上看,这座城市非常美.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>条件状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Given</strong> another chance, I will do better
如果再给我一次机会,我会做的更好.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>让步状语</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Exhausted</strong> by the working, they went on studying at night
尽管工作已经很累了,他们还是坚持在晚上学习.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-753-动词不定式" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#753-动词不定式"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.5.3 动词不定式</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">形式</p>
<p dir="auto">肯定式: <strong>to+动词原形</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">否定式: <strong>not to+动词原形</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center"></th>
<th align="center">主动</th>
<th align="center">被动</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">一般式</td>
<td align="center">to do</td>
<td align="center">to be done</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">进行式</td>
<td align="center">to be doing</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">完成式</td>
<td align="center">to have done</td>
<td align="center">to have been done</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">完成进行式</td>
<td align="center">to have been doing</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>动词不定式的句法作用</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作主语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>To learn</strong> is very important
学习非常重要.</li>
<li><strong>To drive</strong> in the right is not allowed here
右驾在这里不被允许.</li>
<li><strong>To go to college</strong> is a good idea.
去上大学是一个好主意.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">注意</p>
<p dir="auto">①不定式<strong>作主语</strong>时, 可置<strong>句首</strong>;
②如果过长,可采用作<strong>形式主语</strong>, 不定式<strong>后置</strong>的结构</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>结构1
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>it is/was +adj. +to do</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It was difficult to answer the question.
很难回答这个问题.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>it is/was+n. +to do</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It's a big house to clean.
有个大房子要清理.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>结构2
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>it is/was tadj +for something/somebody+to do</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It is necessary for this door to be locked.
锁门很重要.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>it is/was+adj +of sb+to do</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It is very kind of you to help me.
能帮我你太好了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>结构3
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>n.+adj +to do</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He was ashamed <strong>to speak</strong> to her again.
再次和她说话,他感到很羞愧.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作表语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The most important thing is not <strong>to give up</strong>.
最重要的事情是不要放弃.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>做宾语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I want <strong>to swim</strong> in the pool.
我想在泳池游泳
The question was difficult <strong>to answer</strong>.
这个问题很难回答.
A good translator is hard <strong>to find</strong>.
很难找到一个好的翻译.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作定语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Give him an ornament <strong>to polish</strong>.
给他件装饰品擦亮</li>
<li>I need a volunteer <strong>to take</strong> the minutes.
我需要一位志愿者做记录.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>做状语</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>表目的</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The officer returned <strong>to help</strong>.
工作人员返回来帮忙.</li>
<li>He will complete the mission <strong>to set</strong> an example.
他会完成任务,做表率.</li>
<li>I am going to the store <strong>to buy</strong> a 100-watt light bulb.
我打算去商店买一个100瓦特的灯泡.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>表原因</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>My parents will be happy <strong>to meet</strong> you.
见到你我父母很开心.</li>
<li>He was ashamed <strong>to speak</strong> to her again.
再次和她说话,他感到很羞愧</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>常见带to不定式</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">英文</th>
<th align="center">中文</th>
<th align="center">英文</th>
<th align="center">中文</th>

<th align="center">中文</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">afraid</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">amazed</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">anxious</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">ashamed</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">bound</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">careful certain</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">content</td>
<td align="center"></td>

<td align="center"></td>

<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">eager</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">eligible fortunate</td>
<td align="center"></td>

</tr>

</tr>

</tr>

<td align="center">ready</td>
<td align="center"></td>

<td align="center"></td>
