<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">sorry</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">surprised</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">like</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">love</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">prefer</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">begin</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">start</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">agree</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">try</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">attempt</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">choose</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">continue</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">intend</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">propose</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">desire</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">wish</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">want</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">hate</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">dislike</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">hope</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">expect</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">promise</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">refuse</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">fear</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">remember</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">forget</td>
<td align="center"></td>
<td align="center">learn and offer</td>
<td align="center"></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>省略to的不定式</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>感官动词后</strong> see,hear,feel, watch 等.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I felt her heart beat.
我感觉到她的心跳.</li>
<li>I saw it happen.</li>
<li>I watched it happen.</li>
<li>I'll have her copy the document right away.</li>
<li>Our boss let us leave early.</li>
<li>That film made me cry.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>用于被动语态时不定式符号to要添加</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>①使役动词:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>make,let,have 等后作宾补时 <strong>省略to</strong>;  动词help后作宾补语的to可带可不带.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">②当两个或两个以上的动词<strong>不定式并列使用时</strong>, 只有<strong>第一个不定式前带to</strong>, 后面的<strong>省略to</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I often help my friends( <strong>to</strong> )to buy food on the Internet.
我经常帮我的朋友在网上买食物.</li>
<li>The college's aim is <strong>to</strong> help students (<strong>to</strong>)achieve their aspirations
大学意在帮助学生实现志向.</li>
<li>I want <strong>to</strong> lie down <strong>and</strong> sleep.
我想躺下睡觉.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-总结一-动名词与现在分词的区别" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#总结一-动名词与现在分词的区别"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><strong>总结一 动名词与现在分词的区别</strong></h4>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103010527690.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103010527690.png" alt="image-20201103010527690" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作表语</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>现在分词作表语主要用以<strong>说明主语的性质</strong>, 不能与主语换位置.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The story is interesting.</li>
<li>不可改为: Interesting is the story.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>动名词与主语指的是同一件事</strong>此时系动词相当于"是", 通常把主语和表语的位置互换, 语法和意思不变.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>My hobby is swimming.</li>
<li>可改为: Swimming is my hobby.</li>
<li>即: 可将原句中的主语与表语位置互换.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>作定语</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①<strong>动名词</strong>修饰名词时主要表示该名词的<strong>用途</strong>;</p>
<p dir="auto">②<strong>现在分词</strong>修饰名词时<strong>状态或动作</strong>等.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>a swimming boy</strong> 和 <strong>a swimming suit</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>①现在分词 swimming表示被修饰名词boy的动作.即: a boy who is swimming</li>
<li>②动名词"游泳衣". 即: a suit for swimming, 表示 suit 的用途.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>a sleeping child</strong> 和 <strong>a sleeping car</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>现在分词: "—个正在睡觉的孩子"即 a child who is sleeping,表被修饰名词chid正处于的状态;</li>
<li>动名词: "卧车(被用来睡觉的车厢),即 a car which is used for sleeping,表car的用途.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-总结二-现在分词与过去分词的区别" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#总结二-现在分词与过去分词的区别"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><strong>总结二 现在分词与过去分词的区别</strong></h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">①现在分词表<strong>主动或正在进行.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">②过去分词表<strong>被动已完成</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the <strong>rising</strong> sun 正在升起的太阳
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the <strong>risen</strong> sun 升起的太阳</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>falling</strong> leaves 正在落的叶子
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>fallen</strong> leaves 落下叶子</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>boiling</strong> water 正在沸腾的水
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>boiled</strong> water 烧开了的水</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-总结三-动名词与动词不定式的区别" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#总结三-动名词与动词不定式的区别"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><strong>总结三 动名词与动词不定式的区别</strong></h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">有些动词后跟动名词和不定式均可, <strong>意义差别不大.</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>begin, continue, hate, intend, like, love, prefer, start</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">有些动词后面跟<strong>动名词</strong>和<strong>不定式</strong>均可, 但<strong>意义差别较大</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>① <strong>forget to do sth.</strong> 表示忘记要去做某事</li>
<li>② <strong>forget doing sth.</strong> 忘记做过某事</li>
</ul>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">英文</th>
<th align="center">中文</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">forget to do sth</td>
<td align="center">表示忘记要去做某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">forget doing sth</td>
<td align="center">忘记做过某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">remember to do sth</td>
<td align="center">记得要去做某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">remember doing sth</td>
<td align="center">记得做过某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">stop to do sth</td>
<td align="center">停下来去做另外一件事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">stop doing sth</td>
<td align="center">停下正在做的事情</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">regret to do sth</td>
<td align="center">遗憾要去做某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">regret doing sth</td>
<td align="center">遗憾做过某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">try to do sth</td>
<td align="center">努力做某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">try doing sth</td>
<td align="center">试验做某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">mean to do sth</td>
<td align="center">打算做某事</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">mean doing sth</td>
<td align="center">意味着…</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-总结四-现在分词作定语" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#总结四-现在分词作定语"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><strong>总结四 现在分词作定语</strong></h4>
<p dir="auto">现在分词作定语,我们必须注意以下三点:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>两个动作是一前一后发生的, 用<strong>定语从句</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The teacher criticized the student having broken the window. ( X )
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The teacher criticized the student who had broken the window.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Do you know anyone having lost a car? ( X )
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Do you know anyone who have lost a car?</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>动词是 be 动词, 用<strong>定语从句</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Anybody <strong>being</strong> outside after ten o clock will be criticized. ( X )
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Anybody <strong>who is</strong> outside after ten o' clock will be criticized.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>经常性动作, 用<strong>定语从句</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The boy <strong>bringing</strong> us milk <strong>everyday</strong> is my brother. ( X )
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The boy <strong>who brings</strong> us milk <strong>everyday</strong> is my brother.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-总结五-现在分词作状语" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#总结五-现在分词作状语"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><strong>总结五 现在分词作状语</strong></h4>
<p dir="auto">现在分词作状语,我们必须注意以下四点:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>时间</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①<strong>同时发生</strong>时, 用一般式</p>
<p dir="auto">②<strong>先于谓语动词的动作</strong>时, 现在分词要用<strong>完成式</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The secretary <strong>worked</strong> late into the night, <strong>preparing</strong> a long speech for the president.</li>
<li>He <strong>sent</strong> me an E-mail, <strong>hoping</strong> to get further information.</li>
<li><strong>Having suffered</strong> from heart trouble for years, Professor White <strong>has to take</strong> some medicine with him whenever he goes.</li>
<li><strong>Having finished</strong> his homework, the boy <strong>went out</strong> to play football</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>主语</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①现在分词作状语时,其<strong>逻辑主语</strong>与<strong>句子主语</strong>必须<strong>保持一致</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">②如果<strong>不一致</strong>, 分词应有自己的逻辑主语 ,构成<strong>独立主格结构</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Looking out of</strong> the window of our hotel room, we could see lots of mountains around.</li>
<li>They came into the classroom, <strong>talking and laughing</strong>.</li>
<li>Mr.Smith <strong>being absent</strong>, the meeting had to be put off.</li>
<li>It <strong>being</strong> a fine day, we all wanted to go outing.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">现在分词作状语时,前面<strong>可用从属连词</strong> when, while, once 等连词.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>When</strong> talking to you, I always feel happy.</li>
<li>Be careful <strong>while</strong> crossing the street.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">现在分词作状语时与主语之间<strong>不能有并列连词</strong> or, and, but.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Having been told many times, <strong>but</strong> he still couldn 't understand it. ( X )</li>
<li>Having been told many times, he still couldnt understand it. ( v )</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103210351090.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103210351090.png" alt="image-20201103210351090" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-76-动词语法---虚拟语气" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#76-动词语法---虚拟语气"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.6. 动词语法 - 虚拟语气</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">语气</p>
<p dir="auto">①语气是动词的一种形式;</p>
<p dir="auto">②分为<strong>陈述语气</strong>、<strong>祈使语气</strong>以及<strong>虚拟语气.</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>陈述语气</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①陈述语气用来<strong>阐明事实、询问问题、表达意见.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">②<strong>任何动词的时态</strong>都可以用在陈述语气中</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I saw something today that really annoyed me.
我今天看见了一些让我非常生气的东西.</li>
<li>That is a beautiful painting.
那是一幅漂亮的画作</li>
<li>How much wood does a woodchuck chuck?
如果土拨鼠会扔木头那它会扔多少木头?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>祈使语气</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">祈使语气表示命令或请求</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Keep reading.
接着读.</li>
<li>Do not forget your homework.
别忘了你的作业.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">虚拟语气</p>
<p dir="auto">①有<strong>条件</strong>的或<strong>想象</strong>的场景.</p>
<p dir="auto">②<strong>与现实情况相反</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">③表达<strong>主观愿望强烈</strong>时.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>If I were</strong> a rich man, then <strong>I would</strong> have all the money in the world.
如果我是一个有钱人,我就会拥有世界上所有的钱</li>
<li><strong>Had</strong> the man <strong>been</strong> <strong>driving</strong> carefully, he <strong>would</strong> not <strong>have</strong> <strong>crashed</strong> into the
如果这个人开车时谨慎点,那他就不会撞上树了.</li>
</ul>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>if 引导非真实条件句 (必须背熟)</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center"></th>
<th align="center">主句谓语动词</th>
<th align="left">从句谓语动词</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center"><strong>与现在相反</strong></td>
<td align="center">should/would/might/<strong>could+do</strong></td>
<td align="left">①<strong>一般过去时</strong><br>②<strong>be动词用were</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><strong>与过去相反</strong></td>
<td align="center">should/would/might/<strong>could+have done</strong></td>
<td align="left"><strong>had done</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><strong>与将来相反</strong></td>
<td align="center">should/would/might/<strong>could+do</strong></td>
<td align="left">① <strong>were to do</strong><br>② <strong>should+do</strong><br>③<strong>动词一般过去式</strong>(be动词用were)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>与现在相反</strong>的情况
If I <strong>read</strong> six books at once, I <strong>would</strong> confuse all the plots and characters.
如果我现在同时读6本书, 我会把所有的情节和人物混淆.
Even if he <strong>had</strong> a million dollars, he still <strong>would</strong> complain about not having enough.
即使他有现在有一百万, 他还是会抱怨钱不够.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>与过去相反</strong>的情况
If her mother <strong>had taken</strong> the doctor's advice, she <strong>would/might have got</strong> well earlier.
如果她妈妈当时采纳了医生的建议,她就会好得更早.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you <strong>had worked</strong> harder, you <strong>would have got</strong> through the exams.
如果你当时努力学习,你当时就会通过考试了.</p>
<p dir="auto">If I <strong>had won</strong> the lottery, I <strong>would have built</strong> a house in the country
如果我当时中了彩票,我当时就会在乡下建一座房子</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表示<strong>与将来相反</strong>的情况
If I <strong>were to win</strong> the lottery, I finally <strong>would buy</strong> a new car.
如果我将来中了彩票,我到时候就会买一辆新车.
If he <strong>were to be</strong> the next Picasso, I <strong>would be</strong> very happy to have known him for so long.
如果我将来成为下一个毕加索,认识他这么长时间我会非常开心.
If he <strong>were</strong> rich, <strong>he'd buy</strong> a house
如果他将来变得富有,他就会买一栋房子.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">注意:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>if 引导真实条件</strong>句时, 不用虚拟语气.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If it <strong>rains</strong> tomorrow, we won' t go to a park
如果明天下雨,我们就不去公园了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">if 引导的<strong>非真实条件</strong>句的<strong>倒装</strong> ( <strong>主谓倒装</strong>—<strong>部分倒装</strong> )</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If <strong>it were to rain</strong> tomorrow, our picnic would be canceled.
变为
<strong>Were it to rain</strong> tomorrow, our picnic would be canceled.</li>
<li>If <strong>it had not been</strong> for the storm we would have arrived in time.
变为
<strong>Had it not been</strong> for the storm we would have arrived.</li>
<li>If <strong>the earth should</strong> stop running, what would happen?
变为
<strong>Should the earth</strong> stop running, what happen?</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>错综时间条件句</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">在虚拟语气中,当动作和主句动作发生的时间不一致,需要根据句意对主从句所采用的虚拟时态进行变化.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If she <strong>had taken</strong> the doctor's advice, she might still <strong>be alive</strong>.
如果她当时采纳了医生的意见,她现在可能还活着.</li>
<li>If I <strong>were</strong> you, I <strong>would have accepted</strong> their terms.
如果我是你,我当时就会接受他们的条件.</li>
<li>If I <strong>hadn ' t stood</strong> under the ladder to catch you when you fell, you <strong>wouldn' t be</strong>
<strong>miling</strong> now.
当你掉下来时,如果不是我在梯子下面把你接住,恐怕你现在就不会笑了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>无 if 引导的虚拟语气</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>含蓄虚拟条件句</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">介词短语;</p>
<p dir="auto">通过上下文推测;</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Without</strong> air, there <strong>would be</strong> no living things.
没有空气,就没有活的物体.</li>
<li><strong>But for</strong> your help, I <strong>couldn t have done</strong> it.
要不是你的帮助,我就不可能完成它.</li>
<li>We didn't know his telephone number, <strong>otherwise</strong> we <strong>would have telephoned</strong> him.
我们不知道他的电话,否则,我们就给他打电话了.</li>
<li><strong>In that case</strong> we <strong>could have achieved</strong> our goal.
要是那样的话我们肯定就达成目标了.</li>
<li><strong>Under that condition</strong> we <strong>could have lived</strong> more comfortably.
如果在那种情况下我们本可以过的很舒适.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>名词性从句中的虚拟语气</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>wish+宾语从句</strong> "希望,但愿</p>
<p dir="auto">①表示对<strong>现在</strong>的虚拟: <strong>过去式</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">②表示对<strong>将来</strong>的虚拟: <strong>“would /could+动原”</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">③表示对<strong>过去</strong>的虚拟: <strong>“had+过去分词”</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I <strong>wish</strong> I <strong>were</strong> a bit taller
我个子再高一点就好了.</li>
<li>I <strong>wish</strong> I <strong>hadn' t eaten</strong> so much
我真希望自己没吃那么多.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>在表示建议、要求、愿望、命令、坚持、想法</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">advise, command, demand, decide, desire, insist, order, prefer, propose, request, require, suggest 等动词后面的宾语从句, 或这些动词的同源名词后面所跟的同位语从句或表语从句中, 从句谓语用 <strong>"should+动词原形"</strong>, <strong>should可以省略</strong>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">I <strong>suggested</strong> that he implement a budget cut in March.
我建议3月他开始缩减预算.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">It will be essential that they be heard.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">I <strong>demand</strong> that you be at school on time.
我要求你按时上学.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">I <strong>recommend</strong> that Sammi do her homework at home.
我建议萨米在家做作业.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">They <strong>insisted</strong> that all swear words be deleted from the article.
他们坚决要求删除文章中所有皙言相关的话语.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意</strong>:</p>
<p dir="auto">当 suggest, insist 等表“<strong>暗示</strong>” “<strong>坚持</strong>”时, <strong>不用虚拟语气</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He <strong>suggests</strong> that I am not suited for the job.
他暗示我不适合这份工作.</li>
<li>He <strong>insisted</strong> that he was innocent.
他坚持说自己是无辜的.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>在 would rather, would(just), as soon, would sooner, would prefer 后的宾语从句.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①对<strong>现在或将来</strong>的虚拟: <strong>did</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">②对<strong>过去</strong>的虚拟: <strong>had done</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>I’d rather</strong> you <strong>came</strong> another time
我宁愿你下次来.</li>
<li>She would rather he <strong>weren’t</strong> so angry.
她情愿他不那么生气.</li>
<li>I would just as soon you <strong>had told</strong> me the truth yesterday.
我宁愿你昨天告诉我真相.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>主语从句的虚拟语气</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>It is+形容词</strong>( important, necessary,good, right, wrong, better natural, proper, funny, strange, surprising) + that 从句中, 谓语动词的用 <strong>( should)+动词原形</strong>. <strong>should 可以省略</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>It is necessary</strong> that the issue be addressed
必须解决这个问题.</li>
<li><strong>It is proper</strong> that law <strong>should govern</strong> any one of the citizens
法律应制裁以下的任何人.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>It' s time that句型</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>一般过去时</strong> 或 <strong>should+动词原形</strong> , 意为 “该做某事了”</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>should 不能省略</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>It is</strong> high <strong>time</strong> you started off
是你该动身的时候了.</li>
<li><strong>It's</strong> high <strong>time</strong> that we left.
是我们该走的时候了.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>状语从句中的虚拟语气</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>if only 从句</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">①对<strong>现在</strong>的虚拟: <strong>过去式</strong>
②对<strong>将来</strong>的虚拟: <strong>would/could+动原</strong>
③对<strong>过去</strong>的虚拟: <strong>had+过去分词</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If only we could just get on and read it and forget about all the other stuff.
要是我们能够继续读下去并且忘记所有其他的员工就好了.</li>
<li>If only I knew the answer, I'd tell you
要是我知道答案,我就告诉你.</li>
<li>If only I had revised more, I would have done better on my exam
倘若我做更多的修正,我考试成绩就会更好.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>as if 从句</strong> “好像”</p>
<p dir="auto">①对<strong>现在</strong>的虚拟: <strong>一般过去时</strong>
②对<strong>过去</strong>的虚拟: <strong>had+过去分词</strong>
③对<strong>将来</strong>的虚拟: <strong>would(could,might)+动词原形</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>He talks <strong>as if</strong> he knew her.
他说话的样子,好像他认识她.</li>
<li>It looks <strong>as if</strong> it might rain.
看起来好像要下雨了.</li>
<li>It was <strong>as if</strong> the world had come to an end.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>情态动词+ have done</strong> “本该做而没做”</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I <strong>shouldn't have interfered</strong>.
我不应该打断. (事实上已经打断了)</li>
<li>You <strong>should have taken</strong> my advice.
你本应该采纳我的意见. (事实上没有采纳)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223423415.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223423415.png" alt="image-20201103223423415" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223507119.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223507119.png" alt="image-20201103223507119" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223743912.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223743912.png" alt="image-20201103223743912" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223929234.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103223929234.png" alt="image-20201103223929234" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/blob/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103012827108.png"><img src="/Eished/wfyyyf_notes/raw/master/王菲英语语法.assets/image-20201103012827108.png" alt="image-20201103012827108" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-八连词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#八连词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>八、连词</h2>
<p dir="auto">We were wet and tired
我们浑身透湿,精疲力竭.
She's very hard-working but not very imaginative.
她工作很努力,但缺乏想象力.
She walked home by herself although she knew that it was dangerous
她一个人步行回的家,尽管她知道那样做很危险.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-81-并列连词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#81-并列连词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>8.1 并列连词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">第一,表示"和,同,或"</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>and和or表示"和;或"
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Televisions and computers are dominating our daily life.(名词+名词)
电视和电脑正在主宰着我们的生活.
I have to shower and change.(动词+动词)
我得去洗个澡,换身衣服.
The photos are black and white.(形容词+形容词)
这些照片是黑白的.
My best friend and my father' s father both come f/ Yales.(句子+句子)
我最好的朋友和我的祖父都来自威尔士.
She got to the door and put the key in the</li>
<li>She came in and took her coat off
她进来,脱掉了大衣.
I got dressed and had my breakfast
我穿好衣服,吃了早饭.</li>
<li>Is it a boy or a girl?
是男孩还是女孩?
There are people without homes, jobs or family.
有人无家可归,没有工作或家庭.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>both…and, either…or…, neither"nor"
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Both men and women have complained about the advertisement
男人和女人都抱怨过这个广告.
Either you leave now or I call the police!
要么你现在离开,要么我就叫警察!
Neither my mother nor my father went to university
我父母都没有上过大学.</li>
<li>I want to visit Andrew as well as Martin
我想去拜访安德鲁,还有马丁.
They visited some factories, hospitals as well as the schoot.'
他们参观了这所学校,还参观了工厂和医院
as well as连接两个井列的名词或代词做主语,谓i
新的名代
Mary as well as her parents likes mug
玛丽和她的父母都喜欢音乐.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>not only… but also不但…而且…
<ol dir="auto">
<li>She not only wrote the text but also selected the illustrations
她不仅写文章而且还挑选插画.(连接两个谓语动词
If this project fails, it will affect not only our department, but also the whole
organization
如果这个项目失败,不仅会影响到我们部门,还会对整个机构产生影响.(连接两
个宾语)
以下结构语法结构不对称
He not only plays the piano but also the violin. (x)</li>
<li>Not only did he turn up late, he also forgot his books.
他不但迟到了,还忘了带书.</li>
<li>Not only you but also he is a students.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">第二,表示转折意义"但是"</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">but</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">She' s very hard-working but not very imaginative.
她工作很努力,但缺乏想象力.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">i had no choice but to sign the contract.
除了签下合同,我别无选择</p>
<p dir="auto">He's anything but mild.
他一点也不温柔.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">not…but</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>This is not caused by evil, but by simple ignorance.
这并不是恶意而为,只是由于无知.
She's not a painter but a musician.
她不是画家而是音乐家.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">however</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>He was feeling bad. He went to work, however, and tried to concentrate.
他感觉不舒服.然而,他还是去上班了,努力集中注意力.
We thought the figures were correct. However, we have now discovered
some errors.
我们认为数字是正确的.但是,我们已经发现了一些错误.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">whereas 与 while</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>We thought she was arrogant, whereas in fact she was just very shy.
我们认为她傲慢,但是事实上她只是非常害羞.
While Tom's very good at science, his brother is absolutely hopeless.
汤姆非常擅长科学,但是他哥哥在这方面完全没戏.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">第三,表示"否则"</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>or
<ol dir="auto">
<li>He must like her, or he wouldn't keep callinng her.
他肯定喜欢她,否则他不可能一直给</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>or else
<ol dir="auto">
<li>We must be there by six, or else we'll miss the beginning.
我们一定要在6点前赶到那里,要不然就会错过开场.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>otherrwise
<ol dir="auto">
<li>I'd better write it down, otherwise I'll forget it.
我最好把它写下来,否则我会忘了的</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">第四,表示因果关系</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>for
<ol dir="auto">
<li>She remained silent, for her heart was heavy and her spirits low.
由于心情沉重情绪低落,她一直沉默不语.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>so
<ol dir="auto">
<li>legs started hurting so I stopped running.
我的腿开始疼痛,因此我停下来不再跑了.
I was lost so I bought a street map.
我迷路了,所以买了一张街道地图.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>hence
<ol dir="auto">
<li>I fell off my bike yesterday, hence the bruises.
我昨天骑自行车摔倒了,所以青一块紫一块的.
The town was built among the hills, hence the name Hilltown.
该城镇修建在群山之中,故取名" Hilltown</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>therefore
<ol dir="auto">
<li>We were unable to get funding and therefore had to abandon the project.
我们无法筹到资金,因此不得不放弃计划.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>thus
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Agriculture has developed rapidly, thus providing light industry with ample
raw materials.
农业迅速发展,从而为轻工业提供了充足的原料.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-82-从属连词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#82-从属连词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>8.2 从属连词</h3>
<p dir="auto">从属连词表示从属关系,可引导状语从句与名词性从句.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="center">状语从句类型</th>
<th align="left">从属连词</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="center">时间状语从句</td>
<td align="left">then, while, as, before, after, immediately</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">地点状语从句</td>
<td align="left">where, wherever</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">原因状语从句</td>
<td align="left">because, in that,snce,as等</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">让步状语从句</td>
<td align="left">although, though, while, however, wh-ever, nomatter wh-等</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">目的状语从句</td>
<td align="left">in order that, so that, in case, for fear that, for the purpose that 等</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">结果状语从句</td>
<td align="left">so that, such that</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">条件状语从句</td>
<td align="left">it, unless, as long as,等</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">方式状语从句</td>
<td align="left">as,asif, as though等</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="center">比较状语从句</td>
<td align="left">than, not so-as, as-as,等</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">时间状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">When did you leave?
你什么时候离开?</p>
<p dir="auto">The phone rang while we were having dinner.
我们吃晚饭的时候,电话响了.
She gave everyone a present before she left.
她离开前给每个人送了礼物.
No one left the room until the talk ended.
谈话结束后人们才离开.
As you get older, moving house gets harder.
随着你变老,搬家变得越来越困难.
Three months after they moved out, the house was still empty.
他们搬出去3个月了,这座房子仍然空着.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意: "一…就" 的英文表述</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">as soon as
He made a phone call to me as soon as he came back.他一回来就给我打了
个电话.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">once
Once seeing it(= Once you see it ) you can never forget it.
见到了就永远不会忘记.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">at the sight/hearing/sound/( bare )thought/idea of
At the hearing of news, he rushed out. 一听到这个消息, 他冲出去了.
At the hearing of the police officers they ran off. 一看见警官,他们便逃
跑了</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">hardly… when-…, scarcely… when, no sooner…than…</p>
<p dir="auto">Hardly had I left home when it began to rain.
我刚刚离开家门,天就下雨了
He had no sooner returned than he bought a house.
他一回来就买了一套房子.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">the moment the minute, the instant the second.
I recognized him the instant/the minute/the moment/the second I saw.
我一看到他,就认出他来了.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">地点状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>I like to have him next to me where i can keep an eye on him
我想让他挨着我,这样我就可以顺便照看他了.
Wherever I go I always seem to meet him
无论去哪儿,我似乎总是能碰见他.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">原因状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Just because I dont complain, people think I'm satisfied.
就是因为我不抱怨,所以大家认为我满意了.
As it was getting too late, I decided to book into a hotel.
因为太晚了,我决定找家酒店投宿.
The research is important in that it confirms the link between aggression and alcohol.
因为它证实了攻击行为和酗酒之间的联系</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">让步状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Although/ Though he is very old, he is quite healthy
他虽然年纪大了,身体还很健康.
Hard as/though he works, he makes little progress
尽管他学习很努力,但几乎没取得什么进步.
Despite repeated assurances that the product is safe, many people have stopped buying it.
尽管已反复保证了该产品的安全性,很多人还是不再购买.
In spite of its election success, the government is still deeply distrusted on
key health and education issues
尽管选举成功,但是在主要医疗教育问题上,政府仍然不受信任.
This job is open to all, regardless of previous experience
这份工作任何人都可以应聘,不管其以前的工作经历如何.
Whether you believe it or not, it's true.
无论你是否相信,这都是真的</p>
<p dir="auto">No matter what happened, he would persist.(=Whatever happened he would persist)
无论发生了什么事情,他都会坚持的.
No matter who you are, you must comply with the low. (=Whoever you are, you must comply with the law.)
不管你是谁,你都需要遵纪守法.
When anyone does something for you, no matter how small, you should say ”Thank you”.
只要任何人替你做了一件事,不管事情多么微不足道,你都应该说声"谢谢".</p>
<p dir="auto">However(=No matter how expensive it might be, I'll buy it
无论它有多贵,我也要买下它.
They'll stand by you even if you don,t succeed
即使你不成功,他们也会支持你.
Even though it's hard work, I enjoy it.
星然工作艰苦,我还是很喜欢.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">目的状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>In order that he should not be late, his mother woke him up at 6.
为了让他不迟到,他母亲六点就叫醒了他.
He walked fast for fear that he should be late
他快走,以防迟到.
He works hard at his lessons so that he could perform in the exams
他努力学习功课,争取考试能获得好成绩.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">结果状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>The camera is so expensive that I can t afford it
这台相机太贵了(以至于)我买不起.
It was very cold, so that the river froze
天气寒冷,河水都结冰了.
Our country has so much coal that she can export large quantities
我们国家的煤炭非常丰富,可以大量出口.
His plan was such a good one that we all agreed to accept it
他的计划太好了,我们都接受.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">条件状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>If we hurry, we may catch the bus.如果赶紧走我们可能赶得上公共汽车.
Bring a map in case you get lost
带张地图吧,以防迷路.
As long as you do that, then the rest is kind of simple and easy
只要你做到了这点,接下来的就顺其自然了.
Nothing will come of it, unless disaster.
此事除了引起灾祸以外不会有什么结果.
He's welcome to come along, provided that he behaves himsel
他只要守规矩就欢迎他来.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">方式状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Eliza remembers everything exactly as if it happened yesterday.
Eza准确地记得所有的事情,仿佛这些事发生在昨天.
When a pencil is partly in a glass of water, it looks as if it were broke
铅笔的一部分置于水中时,仿佛那部分折断了.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">比较状语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">She likes you better than me
她喜欢你胜过喜欢我.
He can run faster than i do
他跑得比我快.
It is not so difficult as you image
它没有你想的那么困难.
Your pen writes as smoothly as mine.
你的钢笔书写起来和我的一样流畅.</p>
<p dir="auto">The more you read, the better you understand
你看的书越多,你懂得就越多.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-九语法补充" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#九语法补充"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>九、语法补充</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-1定语从句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1定语从句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>1.定语从句</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>关系词
<ol dir="auto">
<li>I know the girl. A girl is talking to Tom
=l know the girl who is talking to Tom
我认识那个正在和Tom说话的女孩.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>关系代词
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Einstein, who was born in Germany, is famous for his theory of relativity.
爱因斯坦出生在德国,以相对论著称
John met a woman(who )i had been to school with
约翰遇到的女人是我曾经的同学.
Do you know the girl( who he's talking to?
你认识他正在聊天的女孩吗?</li>
<li>The camera which costs f 100 is over there
花了100磅的相机在那儿.
The bike( which )I loved was stolen
我喜欢的自行车被偷了.
Where's the pencil( which)I gave you yesterday?
我昨天给你的铅笔去哪儿了?</li>
<li>The meeting was put off, which was exactly what we wanted
会议被取消了,这确实是我们所想的.</li>
<li>The little girl whose toy was lost is sad
那个丢了玩具的女孩很伤心.
Students whose grades are low can drop one test score
分数低的学生可以放弃一门成绩.</li>
<li>The woman whom they visited in hospital was an old aunt of theirs
他们去医院看望的人是他们的大姨.
The boy whom you told me about got the best grades in mathematics
你告诉我的那个男孩在数学上取得了最好的成绩.</li>
<li>I didn't like that girl( that )you brought to the party
我不喜欢你带来聚会上的那个女孩.
The university( that )she likes is famous
她喜欢的大学非常有名.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-2关系副词" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#2关系副词"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>2.关系副词</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>1
<ol dir="auto">
<li>July and August are the months in which most people go on holiday.
=July and August are the months when most people most go on holiday.
七月和八月是大多数放假的月份.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>2
<ol dir="auto">
<li>This is the shop in which I bought books
-This is the shop where I bought books.
这是我买书的商店.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>3
<ol dir="auto">
<li>a horror film was the reason why I couldn' t sleep last night
昨天晚上睡不着的原因是看了一部恐怖电影.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-3限定性定语从句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#3限定性定语从句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>3.限定性定语从句</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>I know the man who is standing there
我认识站在那里的男士.
I visited the town which you told me about
我参观过你告诉我的小城.</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-4非限定性定语从句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#4非限定性定语从句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>4.非限定性定语从句</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">1</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">My new books, which have black covers, are on the desk.
我的新书是黑色封面的,在桌子上.
My bicycle, which I've had for more than ten years, is falling apart.
我的自行车已经有10年了,现在散架了.</p>
<p dir="auto">Ive just come back from London, where my sister lives.</p>
<p dir="auto">我刚从伦敦回来,那是我姐姐住的地方.
Yesterday I met a woman, whose skirt is very shinny.
昨天我见到一位女士,她的裙子非常闪亮</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">2</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>There were a lot of people at the party, many of whom I had known for
years
有很多人在聚会上,其中有些人我认识了很多年了.
He carried vases, many of which were broken
他带了很多花瓶,许多都破了.
He had thousands of books, most of which were destroyed
他有很多书,许多都被毁坏了.
He picked up a handful of stones, one of which was sharp
他见了一把石头,有一个很锋利.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-5that-和-which-的区别" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#5that-和-which-的区别"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>5.that 和 which 的区别</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>只用 which的情况</li>
<li>只能用that的情况
<ol dir="auto">
<li>All that can be done has been done.
所有能做的事情都已经做完了.
Rescuers are doing everything that they possibly can to free the trapped people.
救援人员尽他们所能解救被困人员.
Everything that is in this room belongs to him.
这个房间里面所有的东西属于他</li>
<li>When people talk about Hangzhou, the first that comes to mind is the West Lake
人们提起杭州时,首先进入脑海的便是西湖.</li>
<li>This is the very best present that I,ve ever had
这是我有过的最好的礼物.
It was the only thing that i could do under the circumstances
在这种情况下这是我唯一能够做的.</li>
<li>Who is the boy that is standing there?
站在那儿的那个男孩是谁?</li>
<li>They talked about the persons and things that they remembered at college.
他们谈论着他们所能记起的大学时的人和事.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-6名词性从句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#6名词性从句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>6.名词性从句</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">主语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">That we were late to class really upset the teacher.
我们迟到让老师很失望.
The fact that we were late to class really upset the teaser
我们迟到这件事让老师很失望.
How the boy behaved was not very polite
这个男孩表现的不是很有礼貌.
When he will be there is unsure
他什么时候来不确定.</p>
<p dir="auto">What she wrote surprised her family
她写的东西使她的家人很惊讶.
Whoever thought of that idea is a genius
有那样想法的人是天才.
Whichever restaurant you pick is fine with me.
你挑哪个饭店都可以.</p>
<p dir="auto">注意:
It is immediately clear whether the financial crisis will soon be over</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">宾语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">She didn' t realize that the directions were wrong
她没有意识到方向是错的.
He didn't know why the stove wasnt working
他不知道为什么火炉不能用.
They now understand that you should not cheat on a test
他们现在明白了不该在考试中作弊.
On weekends, we can do whatever we want
周末,我们可以做任何我们想做的事情.
I am not interested in whatever the teacher says
我对老师说的不感兴趣.</p>
<p dir="auto">注意:</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">同位语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">The beast, a lion, was starting to show interest in rabbits.
那只野兽一狮子开始对兔子感兴趣.
The insect, a large cockroach, is crawling across the kitchen table.
那个一只大限过了房的桌子</p>
<p dir="auto">The belief that students can become independent learners is common
among teachers
学生可以成为独立的学习者,这样的想法在老师间很普遍
Our knowledge that students can become independent learners drives
our work
我们的理解:学生可以成为独立的学习者促进我们工作.
The issue whether it is right or wrong depends on the result
这个问题是对还是错要看结果.(不可以引导同位语从句)</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">表语从句</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>My greatest asset is that I am a hard worker
我最大的财富是我是一个努力的工人.
His excuse was that he had forgotten to set his alarm
他的借口是他忘记设置闹钟.
The question is whether the camping is worth going
问题是值不值得去野营.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-7其他语法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#7其他语法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>7.其他语法</h3>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-一强调句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#一强调句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>一.强调句</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>it is/was… that/who
<ol dir="auto">
<li>基本结构
<ol dir="auto">
<li>陈述句: I met him yesterday in the market.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>1
<ol dir="auto">
<li>含有not…untl的句子的强调形式
直到1911年才发现了第一种维生素
The first of the vitamins was not identified until 1991</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>强调句与其他从句的区分
<ol dir="auto">
<li>It is known to all that China has many places of interest
It was his sister who won the 3 in the campaign</li>
<li>It was in the class room that he lost his books
It was the class room where( in which) he lost his books.</li>
<li>It was in the morning when he woke up
It was in the morning that he woke up</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>2
<ol dir="auto">
<li>I do agree with your opinions.
我同意你的观点
Please do come and take part in the game
请一定来参加比赛.
She did work hard this semester.
她这学期确实非常努力.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-二倒装句" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#二倒装句"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>二.倒装句</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">部分倒装</p>
<p dir="auto">否定副词位于句首时</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">I shall never love him
Never shall I love him
我永远不会爱上他.
Hardly anyone came
Anyone hardly came
没人来.
One seldom hears a politician say sorry.
Seldom does one hear a politician say sorry.
从来没听过一个政客说过抱歉.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">He didn t leave the room until the rain stopped.
Not until the rain stopped did he leave the room.
雨停了之后他才离开这房间.</p>
<p dir="auto">I did not realize my wallet was missing until I got home
Not until I got home did I realize my wallet was missing
到家我才发现我的钱包丢了</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">They had no sooner started their walk than it started to rain.
No sooner had they started their walk than it started to rain
他们刚开始散步就下雨了.
I had hardly arrived there when I was called back to the head office 100
niles away
Hardly had I arrived there when I was called back to the head office 100
miles away
我刚到那里就被打电话叫回100英里外的总部
I had scarcely sat down when the doorbell rang.
Scarcely had I sat down when the doorbell rang.
我刚坐下门铃就响了.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">On no account should the house be left unlocked
绝对不能不锁门就离开.
In no way do I agree with what you re saying
我绝不同意你说的.</p>
</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">2</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>I' d seen her flat did I understand why she wanted to live there.
Only when we d all arrived home did I feel calm.
Only by working extremely hard could we afford to eat.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">3</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>The girl was so beautiful that nobody could talk of anything else
So beautiful was the girl that nobody could talk of anything else.
这个女孩如此漂亮以至于没人会谈论其他的内容.
The food was so delicious that we ate every last bite
So delicious was the food that we ate every last bite.
食物太好吃了我们吃的一点都不剩.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">4</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Not only is he a teacher, but he is also a musician
他不仅是一位教师,而且是一位音乐家.
Not only is he difficult to understand, but he is also funny
他不仅很难搞懂,而且他很有超.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">5</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>If I were you, I wouldnt do it.
Vere I you, I wouldnt do it.
如果我是你,我就不会这么做.
If I had understood the problem, I wouldn t have made those mistakes.
Had I understood the problem, I wouldnt have made those mistakes.
如果我理解这个问题,我就不会犯这么多错误.
If you should need a hand, I will be more than happy to help you
Should you need a hand, I will be more than happy to help you.
如果你需要帮助,我非常高兴能帮你.</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-三完全倒装" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#三完全倒装"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>三.完全倒装</h4>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>1
<ol dir="auto">
<li>There is a good restaurant nearby
附近有一家餐馆.
Here comes the bus
公共汽车来了.
Here are the books that I don' t need anymore
这有一些我不需要的书.
[注意]
(1)
Here is coming the bus.(×)
(2)
Here he is.他来了.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>2
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Round the corner came the postman
邮递员从街角过来了.
On the doorstep was a bunch of flowers
门口台阶上放着一束花.
Below me was the beautiful scenery I had been told about
我被告知我下方有美丽的景色.
In the distance could be seen the purple mountains
远处可以见到紫色的山.
[注意]</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ol>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>
